Liang treated him with generosity and did not discriminate against him. Unexpectedly, he has been acting mysteriously recently, traveling between Yuguan and Beidaihe, inciting the army, and intending something. Brigade Commander Ma Tingfu, Regiment Commanders Meng Baifu and An Fukui, stationed in Linyu, were ignorant of righteousness and were deceived by him. Commander Yu Xiaohou has now discovered this and secretly reported it to the headquarters. On the cold day, he and Commander Yu jointly arrested Tao Dunli, Ma Tingfu, Meng Baifu, An Fukui, etc. separately in Yuguan and Beidaihe and detained them all. A military law conference is now being organized to conduct a strict interrogation to clarify Tao's background and the source of his money. The Northeast Army has always been known for its unity. If this incident is realized, it will not only disrupt military discipline but also become a laughing stock for foreigners. Fortunately, Xiaohou considered it carefully and handled it promptly, eliminating the invisible hidden dangers for the Northeast and adding great glory to the soldiers. On that day, Heaven was tired of chaos, and it was raining heavily. Without harming a soldier or breaking an arrow, the ringleaders were captured, and the evil spirit was immediately dispelled. It can be seen that those who have the Tao receive more help, and those who lose the Tao receive little help. The news from afar is deeply afraid of being untrue, so I send this telegram to inform you. Zhang Xueliang seal (19th)

Details of the Central Army's Recapture of Jinan

Jinan Correspondence: Since Han Fuqu abandoned Jinan on June 25th and led his troops to retreat along the Jiaoji Railway, Jin army generals Zhang Yinwu, Feng Pengzhu, Zhuan Zuoyi, Li Shengda, Li Fuying, and others led their troops into Shandong, reaching as far south as Qufu and as far east as Zuoshan. Unexpectedly, in less than two months, the Central Army launched a counter-offensive from the Jinpu Railway, and the situation of the war changed suddenly. As Chiang Kwang-nai, Tsai Ting-kai, Chen Cheng, and other armies successively entered Jinan, the two-way battle came to an end. However, Shandong has been caught in a military sphere for several months, the people have been displaced, commerce has stagnated and declined, and the original vitality has been lost. The following is a description of the Jin army's withdrawal and the Central Army's entry into Jinan:

The Battle Situation Before the Jin Army's Withdrawal: The Central Army's counter-offensive from the Jinpu Railway was divided into three routes. Liu Zhi, the commander-in-chief of the Second Army Corps, was the commander-in-chief. The 11th Division under Chen Cheng and the 13th Division under Xia Douyin were responsible for the front of the Jinpu Railway. The teaching division under Feng Yipei was responsible for the left wing, and the 61st Division under Chiang Kwang-nai and the 60th Division under Tsai Ting-kai were responsible for the right wing. On July 9th, Liu Zhi arrived in Zou County to command the various armies to begin their northward attack. At that time, the troops defending Qufu were the 38th Brigade under Lu of the 13th Division under Xia Douyin, and the troops defending Yanzhou were the 64th Division under Ma Hongkui. The 11th Division under Chen Cheng of the frontal army was ordered to lift the siege of Qufu first. From the 10th, the two sides fought fiercely for many days in the area of ​​Konglin Sishui, Dongjiazhuang, Tuogou, Dongdacheng, and Wusuncun. On July 29th, Chen Cheng's troops advanced eastward from Wangcun, detoured to Sishui, and captured Dongshilai. A part of the troops advanced from Sishui to Yaoshan Pass Loude. On August 4th, they occupied Dawenkou and Nan Yi. The troops on the left wing went out of the road, attacked Daxinzhuang, Xiaoxinzhuang, Huangcaoling, Hongling, Wangjiatang, and Fenghuangshan from Xiaoyandi and Taipingdian, and detoured to attack Jieshou. At that time, the two divisions of Chiang Kwang-nai and Tsai Ting-kai of the right-wing army were transferred to the Jinpu Railway, bypassed Qufu, and also arrived at the right side of Dawenkou on August 4th and continued to advance north. On the 6th, they besieged Tai'an, and on the 10th, they occupied Laiwu. Then they divided into three routes and advanced north. One route went from Laiwu to Qingshiguan, one route advanced along the railway line, and one route attacked Jinan from the back road of Tai'an (this road is the old road that Li Jicai's troops used to attack Baliwa when Zhang Zongchang supervised Shandong in the 14th year of the Republic of China). The troops of Feng Yipei and others on the left wing also bypassed Wenshang and Feicheng and occupied Dongping and Dong'a. While encircling the Jin army in Wenshang and Feicheng, they attacked Changqing. The Jin army defending the Wen River, because the left and right wings of the Central Army had approached Jinan, fearing that their retreat would be cut off, ordered a retreat to the north. However, due to continuous heavy rain, the Wen River was very turbulent. When retreating, the soldiers all passed through the Dawenkou Railway Bridge. Before they had finished retreating, they hastily blew up the railway bridge, resulting in many soldiers falling into the river and being killed by the explosion. There were still thousands of Jin soldiers and more than a thousand civilians on the south bank of the Wen River. Except for those who jumped into the river, the rest were captured by the Central Army. A large number of guns and ammunition and more than fifty cars were abandoned. Because the heavy rain continued and the Wen River became more turbulent, it was difficult to cross the river, so the Central Army did not actively pursue. On August 11th, most of the Central Army had arrived on the south bank of the Wen River, and Liu Zhi himself also arrived. Then he issued a general attack order for each route. On the 13th, the 11th Division under Chen Cheng captured Jieshou, and the 8th Brigade Commander Mao Weisou of the 61st Division also advanced to the Great Wall Ridge from a small road. After two days and nights of bloody fighting with the Jin army, they occupied Zhonggongzhen, only fifty miles away from Jinan, on the evening of the 13th. On the 14th, they advanced north from Zhonggong to Dajiangou and fought fiercely with the Jin army. At the same time, Chen Cheng's troops captured Zhangxia Station, and the teaching division under Feng Yipei on the left wing also arrived at Chenjiafanpu in Changqing. The Jin troops on all routes were cut into several sections and lost contact. The Central Army was able to approach Jinan, and the Jin troops also retreated to the north.

The Jin Army's Withdrawal from Jinan: After the Jinpu Railway military operation was launched, the Jin army also worked very hard in the battle. However, because they initially received news of the Central Army's counter-offensive, the Central Army's actions were secret, and they could not determine the location of its main force. After many days, they still did not see the Central Army attacking north, thinking that the Central Army might be bluffing and not actually coming north. Therefore, they arranged defensive works along Sishui, Yaocun, and Wenshang, and withdrew all the troops that had attacked Qufu and Yanzhou, and changed to a defensive posture. The 18th Army under Qin Shaoguan was also transferred from the Jinpu Railway to the Jiaoji Railway to help in the battle. When the Jin army's left-wing large detour on the Jiaoji Railway was successful and advanced to Zuoshan, the news that Feng Yipei's troops of the Central Army had occupied Dong'a and Dongping on the Jinpu Railway had arrived. Before long, the news that Tai'an was besieged and Laiwu was lost came one after another. The Jin army then changed the Jiaoji Railway to a defensive posture and urgently transferred the 5th Army under Li Fuying and the 9th Army under Feng Pengzhu to the Jinpu Railway to support. After the transportation was completed, Jieshou was lost, and the large force of the Central Army had approached Jinan. They immediately ordered the 5th Army under Li Fuying to rush to Zhonggong to block the Chiang Kwang-nai's troops of the Central Army who were coming north from a small road. When Yan Xishan heard that the war on the Jinpu Railway was urgent, he secretly arrived in Jinan by special train from Taiyuan at 3:00 a.m. on the 12th and convened a meeting in Jinan with Zhang Yinwu, Zhuan Zuoyi, Feng Pengzhu, and Li Fuying. At that time, he thought that Jinan was very important. If it was abandoned, he was afraid that Zhang Xueliang would send troops and that Pingjin would not be guaranteed. Therefore, he decided to defend Jinan to the death. Yan Xishan also issued a very strict order, "No matter whether officers or soldiers retreat, they will all be shot." On the 14th, Zhonggong was lost again. At 7:00 a.m. on the same day, ten planes of the Central Army flew to Jinan and dropped bombs. Three bombs fell on the provincial government, one fell on the security team, killing two soldiers and wounding eight, one fell on the military band, killing one soldier and wounding two, one fell on the backyard kitchen, killing one cook, and one fell behind the locomotive room at Jiaoji Station, killing three children picking coal and wounding three. A small cloth bag fell at Pan Station, and two soldiers were injured when they opened it to inspect it. One fell on the Public Security Bureau of the first district in the city, injuring one patrol chief and three policemen. One fell in Xian Dong Lane, killing a Zhu woman who had come to Jinan from Dongchang to take refuge. One fell in Cang Lane, killing a Zhou Zhao woman and injuring two children. One fell on Weier Road, killing a woman. As a result, Jinan suddenly entered a state of panic. All the personnel of the agencies fled. Deng Chongxi, the acting chairman of the provincial government, moved out of the provincial government at 11:00 a.m. on the 14th, first went to the Shitaiyan Hotel for two hours, and then moved to the Social Bureau. At this time, the Jin army had prepared for a general retreat. Its Ordnance Depot first crossed the river from Luokou and retreated to Yancheng at 10:00 a.m. on the 14th. The Jin army generals also left their original locations and chose safer locations to avoid bombs. At 5:00 p.m., the Central Army had occupied Dajiangou, and the Jin army issued a general retreat order. The large force retreated from Baliwa, went straight to Luokou along Weiyi Road and over the Tianqiao Bridge, with the north bank of the Yellow River as the destination of the retreat. At the same time, the important people also ordered the station to prepare special trains separately, raising fire and waiting for departure. At 8:00 p.m. that evening, the important people of the provincial government went to the station to board the train in order to go north. However, when they arrived at the station, although the special train was there, the locomotive had been removed by the army. Just then, the rear commander Qin Jianbin received a telegram from Shi Yousan, saying that reinforcements would arrive soon and that they should not leave Jinan lightly. So he invited Deng Chongxi and the important people of the provincial government back to the Municipal Government near the station to observe the situation. On that night, the important people of the Jin side also stopped going north because they had news that reinforcements were coming and added the entire 12th Regiment of the Ninth Army of Feng Pengzhu to Baliwa to resist the Central Army coming north, and ordered the Jinpu Railway to send people to repair the power lines south of Baima Mountain. At 12:00 p.m., the battle situation at the front was actually unsustainable, but there was no definite news that reinforcements were coming. They decided to abandon Jinan. At 3:50 a.m. on the 15th, Song Kebin, the provincial committee member and director of the finance department, Nie Xiangxi, the director of the industry and commerce department, Wang Zhaoxun, the president of the high court, and the directors of various tax bureaus such as Zhu Yanzu, Shi Fengxiang, Liu Yan, Xia Yin, Zhou Shiyouyi, etc., first took the special train of the Fourth Route Army from Jinan to Dezhou. At 4:30 a.m., Gu Renfa's special train opened from Jinan North. Gu himself did not board the train. Those who took the train were Yan Xishan himself and all the personnel of his headquarters. The situation at that time was extremely secret. A stationmaster in Jinan personally saw Yan getting on the train. At 9:30 a.m., another special train opened north, which was Yan Xishan's guard car. At this time, Deng Chongxi received a secret telegram from Shi Yousan. At that time, the secret telegram had been taken to Dezhou by the confidential secretary and telegraph translator on the special train of the Fourth Route Army at 3:50 a.m. At 11:30 a.m., Bi Guangyuan, the secretary-general of the Provincial Committee, was found from a certain place and started to translate it. It was reported that the Central Army had entered the city outside the Xinjian Nanwei Gate. They hurriedly took cars to the station. At that time, there was a special train parked at the station, which was Gu Renfa's special train. Xiong Guanmin of the Provincial Committee and Lu Hongshi, the salt transport envoy, had already boarded the train first. Deng Bi and Qin Jianbin and others were anxious and had no choice but to board the train as well. The other attendants tried to have the railway bureau prepare two iron boxcars to be attached behind Gu's car and open to the north together. Unexpectedly, before the two cars could be attached, the Central Army had arrived at the station. Gu and others were in a very urgent situation and had no choice but to abandon the iron boxcars and hurriedly opened their car to the north. As a result, a part of the provincial government officials were all captured. At that time, the Central Army that first arrived at the station was only about twenty people. They fired two shots to show their power. It was about 12:00 noon. There were still four or five thousand Jin troops at the station, but they were in a panic and fled. Zhuan Zuoyi came to Jinan from Baima Mountain at 3:00 a.m. on the 15th and parked his special train at Dahuai Tree. Zhang Yinwu, Feng Pengzhu, Li Fuying, and others all boarded the train at Dahuai Tree and drove to Jinpu Station at 6:00 a.m. to discuss military affairs on the train. When the Central Army arrived at the station, they hurriedly drove north in the chaos of gunfire at 12:00 noon. It can be said that it was dangerous that they were not captured. Later, a train of the Fourth Route Army came from the Jiaoji Railway and opened from Jinan North. The time was 12:20 p.m. Then a train of supplies, a train of ammunition, a train of the transportation office, and a train of airplanes opened north one after another. Zhang Jianwu, the commander of transportation, was killed by a bomb when he got out of the car to direct the departure of the train. After Wang Yijing, the director of the Jinan Municipal Public Security Bureau, heard the Jin army's general retreat order, he appointed Chief Inspector Dou Shixi to act as the director of the Public Security Bureau. He left the bureau at 3:00 p.m. on the 14th and moved to another place. At 11:30 a.m. on the 15th, someone saw him pass through Weiyi Road by car. At 12:00 noon, Wang heard that the Central Army had entered Jinan and hurriedly took a car to the station, wanting to take Gu Renrenfa's special train to the north. But as soon as he arrived at the station, Gu's car had already left, and the Central Army had also arrived at the station. Wang then took a car through the Jinpu Bridge tunnel in the chaos, went out of Guan Zha Camp, and went to Luokou. Unexpectedly, when he arrived at Sunkong Bridge, the car got stuck in the mud due to continuous white rainy days and could not move. At this time, several soldiers of the Central Army saw the car and had rushed over. Wang saw that the situation was urgent and got out of the car and hid in the valley. Because it was daytime, it was difficult to hide, and he was finally arrested. Liu Xihui, the director of the Finance Bureau who was in the same car with Wang, was shot and killed as soon as he got out of the car. It was also heard that before the Jin army retreated to the south, Song Kebin, the director of the Finance Department of the Provincial Government, borrowed 360,000 yuan from the China Communications Bank, Shanghai Industrial Bank, and Fourth Bank in Jinan.

The Situation After the Central Army Entered Jinan: Before the Jin army had completely withdrawn, Liao Qilong, the battalion commander of the 2nd Battalion of the 16th Regiment of the 8th Brigade of the 61st Division, the vanguard of the Central Army, entered the city from Baliwa through Qianfoshan and from the Nanwei Gate (Xinjian Gate) at 11:40 a.m. on the 15th. A part of them were stationed in the Provincial Government, and a part of them went to the station along Weiyi Road to pursue the Jin army. However, after the Central Army entered the commercial port and arrived at the station, the Jin army had not completely retreated, and conflicts occurred between the two sides. The Japanese residents in Jinan pretended to be panic and gathered at the Gengshen Club, Jinan Hospital, and Ordinary Higher Elementary School to take refuge. At 2:00 p.m., the sound of gunfire was no longer heard in the commercial port area, and the main forces of the 61st Division, 60th Division, and 11th Division of the Central Army entered Jinan one after another. As a result, the Central Army gathered in Jinan. At 2:10 p.m. on the same day, Chiang Kwang-nai, the commander-in-chief of the right wing and the commander of the 61st Division, led all the personnel of the division headquarters and the party affairs personnel sent by the Central Party Department to the war zone from Zhonggong to Jinan. The division headquarters was set up in that place. At 3:00 p.m., Tsai Ting-kai, the commander of the 60th Division, also led the personnel of the division headquarters to Jinan. The division headquarters was set up in the Yanwuting. At 3:30 p.m., Chen Cheng, the commander of the 11th Division, also led the personnel of the division headquarters to Jinan and stayed at the Jinpu Railway Hotel. Chiang Kwang-nai was ordered by Chiang Kai-shek to concurrently serve as the Jinan Garrison Commander and issued a notice to appease the people in the name of the Garrison Commander. On this day, due to the sudden change in the situation, the vehicles on the Jinpu and Jiaoji Railways were completely suspended. The telegraph lines between Jinan and Tianjin were also cut off at 12:30 a.m. on the 15th, and all traffic in Jinan was completely cut off. Only one radio station could communicate with the outside world, but military telegrams were crowded, commercial telegrams were backlogged, and news telegrams could not be sent at all.

War News from Various Routes After the Central Army Entered Jinan: After the Central Army captured Jinan, it continued to advance towards Luokou. At 2:30 p.m. on the 15th, it arrived near various ports. At this time, the special trains of the important people of the Jin side had passed the Yellow River Railway Bridge to the north one after another. However, there were still three or four thousand soldiers and four or five trains of ammunition and supplies south of the railway bridge. Seeing that the pursuers of the Central Army had arrived, they hurriedly went north. The soldiers fired and resisted while crossing the river, resulting in many people falling into the water. One train of ammunition derailed in the middle of the bridge and overturned, and other trains could not go north. As a result, by the morning of the 16th, the Jin army had finished crossing the river. More than a thousand soldiers surrendered and handed over their weapons, and more than twenty trains of ammunition, eighty trains of supplies and military supplies, four airplanes, and three locomotives were abandoned. On the same day, the locomotive was used to haul the ammunition and supply trains to Jinan and parked at the Jinpu Station. After the Jin army abandoned Jinan, the 3rd Army under Wang Jingguo, which was defending the Jiaoji Railway, also concentrated near Zhoucun at the same time and withdrew towards Qingcheng in order to cross the river north from Qingcheng again. As a result, the Jiaoji Railway was restored to Han Fuqu. Most of Han's army entered Qingzhou on the 15th, and Sun Tongxuan's troops advanced from Qingzhou to Zhangdian Village, Pujii Zaoyuan, Mingshui, and other places on the 16th, while Cao Fulin's troops guarded Qingzhou and were responsible for pursuing the Jin army towards Qingcheng. The Jin army in Changqing also retreated north across the Yellow River on the 15th and 16th. The Shandong battle came to an end. However, there were still two regiments of the Jin army in Tai'an City, and there were still two brigades of the Jin army in Wenshang and Feicheng. However, their contact had been cut off, and it was quite difficult to persist. On the morning of the 17th, Tsai Ting-kai and Chen Cheng led their troops north, intending to cross the Yellow River north from Qihe, Luokou, and other places. Chiang Kwang-nai, in addition to leaving a part to garrison Jinan, also advanced towards Luokou. As of the 18th, there was still artillery fire in the Luokou area, and the two armies were fighting across the river. The 2nd Army of the 30th Route of the Jin Army, Shi Fengming's troops in Zhoucun, were defeated by the local militia on the 15th and retreated to Changshan County. Yuan Jufeng, the director of the Zhoucun Public Security Bureau, Li Xiantang, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, and Li Baoheng, the head of the defense group, had a telegram to Jinan on the 17th, reporting everything to Chiang Kwang-nai.

Important People of the Central Army Arrived in Jinan One After Another: After the Central Army recaptured Jinan, important people arrived in Jinan one after another. At 10:30 a.m. on the morning of the 16th, Liu Zhi, the commander-in-chief of the Second Army Corps, arrived in Jinan from Nan Honggou Village in Tai'an with Chief of Staff Liu Yaoyang, Adjutant Wang Zunwu, and personnel from eight major departments. He convened a military meeting at the Jinpu Railway Hotel with Chiang Kwang-nai, Tsai Ting-kai, Chen Cheng, and others to discuss the strategy of crossing the river to pursue the Jin army. The meeting ended at 4:00 p.m. Chiang and Tsai returned to their division headquarters, and Liu Zhi continued to discuss military affairs with Chen Cheng. On the same day, Liu Zhi set up the headquarters of the Second Army Corps in the Municipal Government, and he stayed there. Liu Lianyi, a member of the Provincial Party Affairs Rectification Committee, also came to Jinan from Tai'an and immediately took over the provincial and municipal party headquarters and began to work, and rescued Li Kezhen, the director of the organization department guidance section, and Qiu Ruiquan, the director of the propaganda department

Page 12

and editing section of the Public Security Bureau who had been imprisoned. At 5:00 p.m., Xia Douyin also arrived in Jinan by car from Changqing. At 10:30 a.m. on the morning of the 17th, the reporter went to see Liu Zhi at the headquarters of the Second Army Corps. Liu made the following statement, "When the Jin army took advantage of the fact that the Central Army and Feng Yuxiang's army were fighting fiercely on the Longhai Road, they attacked Jinan. Han Xiangfang (Fuqu) abandoned Jinan and retreated to the Jiaoji Railway because he was outnumbered. At the same time, Ma Shaoyun (Hongkui) also retreated south from Tai'an. This time, our army counter-attacked from the Jinpu Railway and was divided into three routes. Each route had more than four divisions. Each route made rapid progress and occupied Dawenkou on August 4th. The Jin army was in a panic and retreated. Because the Wen River was turbulent, they all had to pass through the railway bridge, resulting in countless people falling into the river. A large number of guns, ammunition, and supplies were abandoned, and more than a thousand people were captured. Because of the continuous heavy rain, our army did not actively advance north. On the 11th, our army issued a general attack order for each route, and Jinan was recaptured in just four or five days. On the morning of the 17th, three or four divisions of our army had crossed the river from Luokou to pursue the Jin army. At the same time, a part of the troops was sent to the Jiaoji Railway to jointly attack the remnants of the Jin army with Han's army. There was still a regiment of the Jin army in Tai'an City, and there were also parts of the Jin army in Wenshang and Feicheng. They have all been surrounded by our army and have sent people to negotiate surrender. It is expected that it will be resolved soon. According to the report of Zhang Huichang, the director of the Aviation Administration, our army's planes dropped bombs in Yancheng and destroyed Zhuan Zuoyi's special train. Only the foremost first-class blue steel car was not bombed. Except for all being destroyed, it is unknown whether Zhuan has been in danger." Also, Qian Dajun, the commander of the Teaching Division, arrived in Jinan at 3:00 p.m. on the 17th and returned to Hankou on the 18th. Han Houqu, the commander-in-chief of the First Army Corps, also came to Jinan from Qingzhou at 1:10 p.m. on the 17th with his Chief of Staff Zhang Yue, Chief of Staff Zhao Guangpei, Operations Section Chief Jia Benjia, and Chiang Bocheng, the chief adviser of the General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force. Regarding the security of Jinan, Liu had appointed his adjutant Wang Zunwu as the director of the Jinan Public Security Bureau. Wang took office at the bureau at 7:00 a.m. on the 18th. Huang Shang, the director of the ordnance factory, was also appointed by Liu Zhi and took office on the 17th. At 8:00 a.m. on the 18th, Liu Zhi received Jinan newspaper reporters at the Second Army Corps Headquarters and gave a lengthy speech. As for the traffic on the Jinpu and Jiaoji Railways, the bridges are being repaired urgently. The Jinpu Railway has a huge break in the Dawenkou Railway Bridge and will be opened in sections first. The Liuhe Bridge on the Jiaoji Railway was repaired at 6:00 p.m. on the 19th and will be opened on the 20th. Kaga Yama Manabu, the Japanese director of the Jiaoji Railway Vehicle Department, Tan Shukui, the deputy director, Cai Guozhao, the director of the Machinery Department, and Deng, the director of the Engineering Department, arrived in Jinan from Qingdao by special train at 12:00 noon on the 19th. As for the Jin personnel who were arrested, they were all imprisoned in the Xincheng Ordnance Factory. It was heard that Wang Yijing, the director of the Public Security Bureau, had committed suicide in the ordnance factory.

The Provincial Government Moved from Qingdao to Jinan: The Shandong Provincial Government moved to Qingdao on June 25th. Now that Jinan has been recaptured, they took a special train from Qingdao at 3:00 a.m. on the 19th. They arrived in Jinan at 7:40 p.m. The members of the committee were acting chairman and director of the civil affairs department Zhu Xi, member and director of the finance department Yuan Jiapu, director of the education department He Siyuan, director of the construction department Chen Luanshu, director of the industry and commerce department Chen Mingyu, director of the mines department Yu Enbo, provincial government secretary-general Liu Fu, civil affairs department secretary-general Ning Kun, and more than fifty personnel from various agencies. Qingdao Mayor Ge Jingen, Jinan Ordnance Factory Director Zhao Yibang, Li Erkang, chief of staff of the General Headquarters of the Suppressing Rebel Army, and all personnel from the provincial and county party headquarters. The provincial government is scheduled to start working on the 20th. (Evening of the 19th)

Singapore

Measures to Prohibit the Import of Chinese Laborers

A Trial Period of Three Months

Only Allowed to Land in Singapore and Penang

Penang Correspondence: The Straits Settlements government announced on July 31st that it would prohibit Chinese laborers from landing on the Malay Peninsula within three months, which has a huge impact on our country's labor sector. The implementation measures are very strict. Singapore is the gateway to the Malay Peninsula, not only a must-pass place for Chinese expatriates from our country to the Malay Peninsula, but also a hub for Eurasian transportation. Now, the import of Chinese laborers is prohibited. It has been announced that all adult Chinese laborers who move from China will be calculated in Singapore. After the calculation, they can be transferred to Penang to land. The work of calculating the number of entries is handled by the Port Service Officer, and one person is sent by the Chinese Protector to help. Laborers who are not allowed to enter other ports other than Singapore and Penang are not allowed to land. Chinese laborers who land in Penang must also be calculated in Singapore. If they do not follow the above measures and attempt to land in other ports, they will be immediately arrested. It is said that the reasons are: (1) The Malay Peninsula is entirely an industrial area, and if the import of Chinese laborers is completely prohibited, it will have an impact; (2) If the shipping companies that travel between Hong Kong, Shantou, and Xiamen stop carrying passengers, they may go bankrupt; (3) At this time of commercial warfare competition, it is difficult to be self-satisfied and not interact with other markets. Due to these three reasons, the Straits Settlements government has stipulated a trial period of three months as a workaround. Each month, 5,000 Chinese laborers are allowed to be imported and distributed to various shipping companies for transportation. However, the losses suffered by the shipping companies due to the ban on Chinese labor are quite large. During these three months of restrictions, in order to prevent losses, they may increase fares in order to make up for their losses. (August 8th)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

County Government Requests Maintenance of Education Funds: The County Education Bureau of this county previously submitted the budget for the county-run middle school, county-run normal school, and primary schools at all levels for the 19th year. It was ordered to review and reduce it. Upon hearing this news, all schools found it difficult to maintain operations and collectively tendered their resignations. The school principals also passed a resolution on this matter in a joint meeting. This matter came to the attention of the county government, which specifically raised it for discussion at the 71st county administrative meeting yesterday (the 21st). It was unanimously agreed that the cost of living has been continuously increasing in recent years, and various school expenses have increased several times compared to the past. If the budget is cut, it will indeed be difficult. It was resolved that the county government would forward the original proposal to the Department of Education, requesting its maintenance to demonstrate understanding and consideration.

Reduction of Administrative Expenses for District Offices: The Civil Affairs Department of this province previously issued regulations on the operation of district offices, stipulating that district administrative expenses should not exceed one-third of the business expenses. It is found that the administrative expenses for district offices in this county were originally set at $250 per month for Grade C districts and $200 per month for Grade D districts. According to the provincial regulations and based on the economic conditions of this county, the monthly expenses for Grade C districts should not exceed approximately $70, and for Grade D districts, approximately $60. The county government will implement the detailed rules for district office operation issued by the provincial government from September 1st, according to Articles 2 and 17 of the issued district operation regulations, appropriately distribute funds, and issue notifications to each district. This was resolved through the county administrative meeting.

Suzhou

Recovered Wounded Soldiers Sent to Beijing to Return to Their Units: Over 300 officers and soldiers who had recovered at the Fifteenth Rear Hospital were sent to Beijing at 5:00 AM yesterday (the 22nd) to return to their units. Before departing, the management committee distributed $8.30 to each person at the station.

Shen Guolin Commits Suicide in an Inn: Shen Guolin, formerly employed at Yu Renhe Grain Store outside Loumen and currently a clerk at the Grain Stabilization Bureau, was 22 years old and resided at No. 2, Mianhua Lane, Pingjiang Road. Due to the pressure of livelihood, he committed suicide by swallowing an anesthetic solution in Room 24 of the Xin Su Tai Inn in Changmen. After being discovered yesterday morning (the 22nd), he was sent to Su Yong Hospital for treatment.

Wuxi

Anti-Smuggling Unit Engages in Fierce Battle with Salt Smugglers: The Second Company of the Seventh Anti-Smuggling Brigade, stationed in Tangkou Town, received a tip on the evening of the 20th that a large group of over 40 salt smugglers, aboard 13 Ningbo open boats, were fully loaded with over 1,000 loads of smuggled salt and were engaged in sales in Jialingtang, on the border of Xiyu, carrying quick-firing guns and Mauser pistols. Upon receiving the report, Company Commander Li Chuquan immediately led a team of elite soldiers to apprehend them the following morning. As soon as they arrived at Xiadian Bridge, the smugglers, seeing the arrival of government troops, immediately laid ambushes and opened fire to resist arrest for a long time without a clear outcome. At that time, patrol boats stationed in Tangkou, upon hearing that government troops had already opened fire, immediately dispatched five boats to assist. Unable to withstand the pressure, the smugglers, led by their leader, began to retreat towards Yuanshan Tang River. Several smugglers were killed on the spot, and countless were wounded. However, all the bodies were seized and taken away. On the official side, Patrol Leader Liu Chun of Patrol Boat No. 6 and Zhang Guoyi, helmsman of Patrol Boat No. 1, died heroically in action after being stabbed by the smugglers' knives. Patrol Leader Ma Hongbin of Patrol Boat No. 7 and Shi Renyi, helmsman of Patrol Boat No. 1, were both wounded in the legs by bullets. Company Commander Li ordered the transfer of the remains of Liu and Zhang back to Tangkou for encoffining, and the wounded Ma and Shi were immediately sent to Puren Hospital in the city for treatment.

Hunan Refugees Cause Disturbances While Passing Through: Since Changsha, Hunan, was ravaged by the Communists, people have been fleeing to various places to survive. The town of Daqiangmen in Wuxi County was visited by over 200 Hunan refugees the other day, entering from Kunshan via Changshu. The leader carried a passport issued by Kunshan County and requested 3.7 shi of rice and $12 from the 12th District. District Chief Tu Keqiang, seeing that the leader was wearing a white gauze long shirt and a gold watch, found it suspicious and immediately gave him $15 to buy rice himself. He also reported to the 11th Sub-bureau of the Houzhai Public Security Bureau and the Chamber of Commerce for temporary vigilance. By the next morning, the refugees had left the town towards Changshu. However, in the afternoon, a large number of refugees carrying firearms arrived in Wengjia Village and Xuedian in the district and caused extensive disturbances. The homes of Weng Wenxiang and a few other families were robbed. Upon receiving the report, the 11th Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau not only dispatched teams to suppress the situation but also reported to the County Public Security Bureau and the County Government for instructions on how to handle the matter.

Dismissal of County Police Captain: Zhu Zhenguo, the Captain of the County Police Brigade, was repeatedly accused by the people to the Provincial Department, resulting in a pile of accumulated cases. The County Government had previously been ordered to investigate. Recently, Ding and others filed accusations with the Civil Affairs Department. After Minister Hu of the Civil Affairs Department sent personnel to Wuxi to secretly investigate and verify the accusations, he specifically instructed the County Government to dismiss Zhu Zhenguo from his post and to hand over the official seals, firearms, ammunition, and files by a specific date. Wang Wei has been appointed to Wuxi to succeed him.

Capture of the Communist Party's Commander-in-Chief of Three Counties: Xia Bingwen, the Captain of the Investigation Team of Jingjiang County, learned that Zhu Deqing, the Commander-in-Chief of the Communist Party in the three counties of Jingjiang, Rugao, and Taixing, and Wan Diyi, the Commander of the Second Route of Jingjiang, had fled to Wuxi due to strict pursuit by the authorities. He immediately reported to the County Government and brought a formal letter to Wuxi. Disguised as a peddler, he carefully investigated at the station and wharves. Yesterday afternoon, he saw Zhu Deqing with his false orderly Zhu Guoxiang, and Wan Diyi with his false orderly Lin Zhuquan, lingering at the station. Captain Xia immediately stepped forward to arrest them. A Browning pistol and 65 bullets were found on Wan Diyi's person. According to their confessions, they were planning to go to Changzhou for activities. They were immediately taken to an inn and reported to the County Public Security Bureau for verification.

Changzhou

Military Police Corps Joint Defense Office Holds Meeting: Jiang Xiaoxian, the Director of the Wuyi Military Police Corps Joint Defense Office (also the Commander of the Gendarmerie Battalion), handed over his position to Wu Chengren, the Commander of the Second Gendarmerie Regiment of the Central Army, who had arrived in Changzhou from Suzhou, according to the regulations of the Joint Defense Office, which stipulated that the Director should be the highest-ranking local military officer. Commander Jiang handed over the position, documents, and other items to Commander Wu and reported to the Capital Garrison Headquarters for record. After taking over, Commander Wu moved the Joint Defense Office to the regimental headquarters in Fangsheng Temple for ease of command. He convened a meeting of representatives from party, government, military, and civilian organizations at 2:00 PM on the 21st to discuss measures for inspecting hotels, ships, postal services, and telecommunications. It was also resolved to request approval from the Commander-in-Chief of the Bandit Suppression in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui provinces to use the official seal.

Director of Cooperation Guidance Arrives in Changzhou: Xu Heling, the Director of Cooperation Guidance of Wujin, appointed by the Jiangsu Department of Agriculture and Mining, arrived in Changzhou from Nantong via Jiangyin on the morning of the 21st. He contacted Wu Zhenya and Ye Tongshan, the guidance officers who had arrived in Changzhou earlier, to discuss everything. He then went to the County Government and the Party Headquarters to discuss office space and funding issues. It was decided that the office would be located in the former Farmers' Association. As for funding, due to the failure to collect the land tax for agricultural improvement, there was no solution. Director Xu went to the province on the 22nd to ask Director He of the Department of Agriculture and Mining for instructions.

Zhenjiang

Zhazeh Station Relocated to Qiaotou: Zhazeh Station, located about nine li from Zhenjiang, has been established for a long time. However, due to its remote location, there are few travelers. On the other hand, Qiaotou Town, between Gaozi and Xiashu, has established San Gao School and a farm, with more frequent travelers. Therefore, the Ministry of Railways ordered the directors of the two railway administrations to immediately relocate Zhazeh Station to Qiaotou to facilitate travel. After receiving the order, the directors are reported to be preparing to abolish Zhazeh Station and establish a new station in Qiaotou Town soon.

Director of Construction Promotes Electric Irrigation: The Construction Department of Jiangsu Province previously received instructions from the Construction Committee, stating that electric irrigation had been piloted near the Qiyan Shuye Electric Plant under its jurisdiction, proving to be beneficial without any disadvantages. Recently, the First Irrigation District Committee was established to promote it vigorously, achieving remarkable results. Therefore, it should be imitated and extensively publicized. After receiving the instructions, the Construction Department specifically instructed the Construction Bureau yesterday to urge local power plants to actively implement the policy to increase agricultural income.

Yangzhou

Dispute Arises During Gambling Arrest: The Fourth Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau in the Fairy Maiden Town of this county received a report at 6:00 PM the other day (the 19th) that people were gathering to gamble in the Dasheng Temple in Hebei. The bureau dispatched police officers to the scene and caught eleven gamblers and three mahjong sets, taking them all to the bureau. Just as they were preparing to hold a preliminary hearing, a mob of several hundred people went to the bureau, swarming inside. The police officers were unable to stop them, and the arrested gamblers were snatched away. Later, Chairman Guan of the Chamber of Commerce intervened to mediate, and they dispersed. It is reported that after the incident, Director Zhang entered the city to report the details to County Magistrate Chen, who is also the Director of the Public Security Bureau, seeking instructions.

Changes in the Commissioner of the Yangzhou Customs: Weng Shuchen, the Commissioner of the Yangzhou Customs, has served in the customs service for 31 years and is retiring according to regulations, receiving a lump-sum performance bonus of 70,000 yuan. Weng has been approved by the General Customs Service to resign. Zhou Ziheng, the Commissioner of the Chongqing Customs, has been transferred to fill the vacancy. Zhou is expected to take office in Yangzhou on September 1st. Before his arrival, the current Deputy Commissioner, Xia Tingyao, will act as his agent.

The Public Finance Construction Bureau Reconsiders Rickshaw Fees: The Public Finance Construction Bureau has been discussing the opinions of rickshaw merchants through assigned representatives. The results are: (1) Rickshaws reporting to the bureau by the 15th (for fees not yet paid from the 3rd) will have late fees waived. (2) If a license is lost, a duplicate license will be issued, with the word "Duplicate" printed on it, for a fee of 50 cents per license. (3) If a metal plate is broken, rickshaw drivers may obtain a new one from the Construction Bureau for 10 cents per plate.

Jiangyin

Fifth District Inspector Investigates Opium Case: The patrol boat of the Fortress Headquarters seized 19 catties of opium at Liuwei Port in the Yangtze River on the 16th and arrested opium traffickers Qiu Zanqing, boatman Pan Rongfu, and waterway police officers Chen Bingquan and Liu Hanbing. Yang, the Commander, and Li, the County Magistrate, jointly held a military trial and telegraphed the Civil Affairs Department for instructions. They received a reply, ordering them to be dealt with severely according to the law. Jiang Chaoxiong, the Fifth District Chief, appointed Tao Fengwei to investigate in Cheng yesterday (the 20th). Tao investigated at the County Government, the County Party Headquarters, and the Chamber of Commerce. The County Government copied a transcript of the confession and brought it to the district headquarters for study. Tao believes that the facts of this case are confirmed and cannot be clarified in a short period of time and require detailed investigation. Consultations with various agencies generally yielded the same results as reported in the newspapers. Tao is scheduled to return to the province on the 21st. The officers of the 20th Squadron of the Water Police Brigade believe that the opium case is of great importance, affecting the reputation of the entire team. They are studying several issues related to this case: (1) Whether military trials can be applied to this case. (2) Whether torture can be used during the preliminary hearing. (3) Whether instruments of torture can be used for public sentencing. (4) Whether confessions obtained under torture can be used as legitimate testimony. (5) Whether torture involves acts of violence, coercion, or fraud. The above-mentioned issues should be judged by the district committee with a legal and fair attitude. In short, the content of this case is complex and difficult to resolve thoroughly.

County Magistrate Li Accused: Wu Zhongxing, a resident of Shizhuang, Taohua Township, in the western countryside, and currently an employee of the County Reorganization Committee, accuses County Magistrate Li Leng of having achieved nothing in his four months of office and of failing to suppress bandits, among other unfavorable public opinions. He has submitted a petition to the Civil Affairs Department requesting his removal and investigation, which has been approved pending investigation and verification by dispatched personnel.

Gaoyou

Sand Community Boat Robbed: A Sand Community boat, which sailed from Shagou to Jieshou the other day (the 18th), was suddenly encountered by more than ten bandits carrying guns near Shibao. The bandits ordered the boat to stop and swarmed aboard to rob it. The boat owner was robbed of more than 200 yuan, the passengers were robbed of more than 800 yuan, and the shops lost silver. The total loss is estimated to be more than 2,000 yuan.

Oath-Taking Ceremony for the Heads of the Education and Construction Bureaus: Sun Weixian, the Head of the Education Bureau, and Zhu Fuzhen, the Head of the Construction Bureau, held a supplementary oath-taking ceremony in the auditorium of the County Government at 9:00 AM today. Approximately 200 representatives from various agencies attended.

Pinghu

Burglary in Tushan Tou, Zhapu: The home of the Qian Guansi clerk in Tushan Tou, outside the West Gate of Zhapu, was suddenly attacked at 1:00 AM last night by more than ten bandits speaking with a northern accent. Armed with knives and clubs, they broke down the door and tied up all the men, women, and children in the family. They lit kerosene lamps and burned the clerk's arms, forcing him to reveal the location of the hidden silver. Unable to endure the pain, he handed over all the 80 silver dollars he had accumulated. The bandits also ransacked the clothes, chests, and baskets. They only left at dawn with whoops and calls. Tushan Tou is located near Zhapu City and has been robbed five or six times.

Dead Body Revived by Electric Shock: At the home of a farmer surnamed Zheng outside the North Gate of Zhapu, the father and son had an argument due to minor family matters the other day, which led the son to commit suicide. He hanged himself in the evening. The family discovered and rescued him, but it was too late. Unexpectedly, last night, there was a thunderstorm. A thunderbolt struck the body of the hanged man and revived him. The whole family was overjoyed and celebrated the revival. The corpse is now moving as usual. When asked about what happened after death, he was completely ignorant. It is often heard that living people die from electric shock, but it has never been heard of a dead body being revived by electric shock. This matter is worth studying by scientists.

Jiaxing

Xupoqiao Town Robbed: Xupoqiao Town in the southern part of Jiaxing is a small market town with rows of shops and a large population. Because of its remote location, there had been no disturbances for decades. But at about 6:00 PM on August 20th, forty or fifty bandits were suddenly discovered patrolling the streets of the town. The townspeople initially did not care because there was no defense by water or land police or self-defense corps, so they had to let nature take its course. After a while, the bandits fired shots to demonstrate their strength and began to guard the town in various directions, starting to rob each household. None of the merchants and residents with some wealth were spared. At the same time, a townsman named Zhang Shenghe was shot by the bandits, and many others were injured with wooden sticks. The robbery lasted three or four hours before they left with their loot. The wounded have been sent to the hospital for treatment. Townspeople Hu Ganqing and Zhou Pengshou went to the city at noon on the 21st to report the robbery to the county government. County Magistrate Jiang, along with the Director of the Public Security Bureau Mo, went to the scene for inspection and prepared to order an investigation.

Hangzhou

Police School Graduates Studying Abroad: In order to train high-level police personnel, the Zhejiang Provincial Government has sent graduates of the Police School to study in Japan and Austria. The first batch of twenty students has already gone to Japan for inspection and returned to Zhejiang. In addition to being assigned to various county police agencies, the Civil Affairs Department has also assigned six students to the Provincial Public Security Bureau. The ten students studying in Austria are also preparing to go abroad. Thirteen measures have been established, temporarily setting half-expenses for studying in Japan and full-expenses for studying in Austria. The duration of the study is one to two years.

The City's Grain Supply Will Stop in Twenty Days: The grain in Hangzhou City is being manipulated by unscrupulous merchants who are refusing to let new rice be unloaded, resulting in a shortage of food for the citizens. According to the grain surplus and deficit report submitted by the Grain Council to the Municipal Government, there were 36,789 shi of grain remaining from the 11th to the 17th of this month, enough to supply the city for twenty days.

Shaoxing

Resolving the Surplus Rice After the Suspension of Grain Sales: The Shaoxing Grain and Wheat Maintenance Association had previously transported over 10,000 packages to Shaoxing for price stabilization sales. Because of the new grain season and abundant harvests, rice prices fell, and there was no need for price stabilization sales. The association decided to suspend sales and distribute the surplus rice to rice merchants for sale. Because the agreed price differed from the market price, it was difficult to persuade people to buy, and the surplus rice has not yet been sold. The association decided that the county should convene a joint meeting of rice merchants from various towns and townships at the County Chamber of Commerce at 11:00 AM on the 23rd to appropriately reduce the price on the spot and instruct each leader to purchase the grain immediately and pay on a daily basis in order to find a solution. County Magistrate Tang sent letters to the rice merchants in various towns and townships yesterday, requesting them to attend the meeting to discuss a solution.

Shangyu

Jailbreaker and Thief Caught: Hu Acai, a habitual thief, escaped from prison in 1928 due to the negligence of former official Zhu. Although a reward was offered for his arrest, he was not caught. In the past two years, the fugitive has committed numerous major crimes in the urban and rural areas. As the arrest became more urgent, he fled to Daoxu in Shaoxing. A few days ago, he went to Xihua Village in Songxia to sell green pears and was spotted by Hu Zhenfan, the squad leader of the County Defense Team stationed in the town. He was arrested and sent to the county government for interrogation. He has now been shackled and imprisoned. The county government has also awarded the squad leader a reward of 20 yuan to encourage him.

Adulterous Woman and Lover Beat Her Husband: Xia Ayu, the wife of Gong Achen, a fried food vendor in the East Gate of the city, has been living with Gong for more than ten years and has given birth to two children. However, this year, Xia Ayu suddenly changed her attitude and became acquainted with Luo Huanwen, an internal affairs officer of the County Public Security Bureau. They went in and out without avoiding the eyes of neighbors and her husband. Achen was afraid of his power as an officer of the Public Security Bureau and could do nothing. At the beginning of this month, Xia secretly ran away and lived with Luo in the Tangzong Temple in the same district, publicly declaring that she had paid 60 yuan to divorce her husband. On the 19th, Achen went to his wife's residence to persuade her to return. After an argument, Xia shouted at the neighbors Ge and tailor Wang, among others, to beat him, causing Achen's head, face, arms, and other parts to bleed profusely. Passersby felt indignant and wrote a complaint on his behalf, requesting assistance from the County Party Headquarters.

Ningbo

Fraud Case Cracked: The Xingyuan Money Shop in Gongqian City was defrauded of over 270 yuan on the 18th of this month by a monk who had returned to secular life, Chen Taoyue, who forged the seal of Chen Lifang of the Chen Shuntai Southern Goods Store in Shenjiamen. The case remained unsolved. Unexpectedly, Chen Taoyue used the forged seal again yesterday to defraud the shop of money. He was recognized by an apprentice from the He Zhenfeng Silk Shop, who reported it to the investigation team, who arrested the fraudster and took him to the team for investigation.

Members of the Chamber of Commerce Take Office: The members of the Committee for Unifying Business Organizations in this city, Yuan Duanfu and eight others, recommended by the Provincial Chamber of Commerce, were approved and appointed by the Provincial Party Headquarters. Yuan Duanfu, Lin Fen, Lin Jianzhong, Yan Su, Zhou Zicai, Yu Huang, Wu Zemin, and Mao Jieying took the oath of office in the auditorium of the County Party Headquarters yesterday (the 19th).

Local News

Wang Jiazhen Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday

Stated that the Northeast's Attitude Remains Consistent

Scheduled to Go to Beijing Tomorrow Evening to Return to Duty

Wang Jiazhen, the Deputy Minister of Foreign Affairs, returned from Liaonan with his family, stopping briefly in Qingdao. He arrived in Shanghai on the Fengtian Maru at 4:30 PM yesterday and landed at the Huangpu Wharf. Those who went to welcome him included Chen Shiguang, the Director of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Deputy Director Liu Yunfang, and over a dozen of Wang's relatives and friends. This reporter interviewed him at his residence yesterday, and his remarks are summarized as follows:

Mayor of Qingdao: Wang said that Hu Ruoyu originally planned to go to Qingdao around the 10th to assume the position of Mayor. At that time, I was waiting for Hu in Huludao to come from Tianjin to go together. Unexpectedly, the Beining Railway was impassable due to flooding. I waited for Hu for a long time without his arrival, so I returned to Yingkou and transferred to Liaonan. Hu is currently handling family affairs in Tianjin and is expected to go to Qingdao soon. When asked if it was true that Zhang Xueming would be appointed as the Qingdao Garrison Commander, he replied that Zhang would accompany Hu south, but the specific position he would hold had not yet been determined.

Attitude of the Northeast: When asked about the recent attitude of the Northeast and when Mayor Zhang would return south, Wang said that he did not want to express any opinions on political issues. All he could say was that the Northeast's attitude has remained consistent. The date of Mayor Zhang's return south is still uncertain. He thought he had already returned to Liaoning with Commander Zhang.

Sino-Russian Negotiations: Wang also said that regarding the Sino-Russian negotiations, he met with the Russian Consul in Liaoning and learned that the progress of both sides was smooth. He spent some time in Liaoning because he was finishing up various unfinished matters from his previous term. He also went to the border between Korea and Yanji to investigate the situation of Korean immigrants in the Northeast. After returning to Liaoning, he hurried south.

Going to Beijing Tomorrow Evening: Wang also said that this time, his wife and maid were not used to sailing. After arriving in Qingdao, they were extremely exhausted and rested at the hotel for four days before coming to Shanghai. He plans to meet with Foreign Minister Wang this morning and take a train to Beijing tomorrow evening to return to duty. When asked about his opinion on the North Daihe news spread by foreign news agencies, he replied that foreign reporters are not familiar with the situation in China and easily spread rumors and make mistakes. Therefore, he strongly advocates that all news should be provided to domestic reporters first and that they should be approached frequently. However, Chinese people often like to be close to foreign reporters, which is very inappropriate.

National Government Telegraph

Urging Chen Xizeng to Take Office

Director Chen Expresses Further Consideration

Chen Xizeng, the newly appointed Director of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (CMSNC), presented his resignation to the National Government after receiving the formal commission, because he deemed that the CMSNC's future was very important, and he was not able to take on such responsibility, and it was inconsistent with his values, and it was incumbent upon him to offer his resignation. It is reported that the Secretariat of the National Government telegraphed yesterday, urging him to take office quickly. The original telegram is recorded as follows:

Telegram from the Secretariat of the National Government: Shanghai Telegraph Bureau forwards to Director Chen Xizeng of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, Please see and consider. The Chairman has instructed that shipping is important and needs to be reorganized urgently. You are expected to take office quickly, endeavor to overcome the difficulties, and there is no need for concern. Secretariat of the National Government.

Chen Xizeng's Talk: A reporter from New Voice News learned of the telegram from the Secretariat, urging Chen to take office quickly, and went to visit Chen to ask for his opinion. According to Chen, he serves the party and the country with a fact-based approach. So long as it benefits the party and the country, he is not be afraid of any difficulties. This time, he has been suddenly appointed as the Director of the CMSNC. However, it is very important, and if he has no confidence in how to fix this, he would be unqualified for this task. In addition, the financial difficulties of the company need to be carefully addressed. Therefore, with the telegram from the National Government, he has to further consider this matter.

Statement from the Transportation Authorities: A reporter from New Voice News in Beijing visited the transportation authorities on the issue of Chen Xizeng's resignation as Director of the CMSNC. According to the person in charge of the Ministry of Communications, the reorganization of the CMSNC cannot be achieved overnight and requires time and careful planning. Chen's resignation is not due to any major reason. He feels that a prolonged delay would bankrupt the company, so he would rather step aside for someone more capable. However, the Ministry has not yet received his official resignation document. Even if Chen insists on resigning, the National Government and the Ministry of Communications will try to retain him. The difficulty of the CMSNC is not in the duties but in the entire economic problem of the company. The organization and content of the CMSNC will be improved. Minister of Communications Wang Boqun has determined that the company will be jointly operated by the government and merchants. As the situation stabilizes, merchants investing in enterprises and the government subsidizing the development of transportation will be able to advance together. Currently, foreign ships are increasingly encroaching on navigation rights in the Yangtze River. If domestic ships are not protected and encouraged, inland waterway rights will be lost to foreigners without a fight. It is also heard that the Ministry of Communications has drafted a plan to reorganize the CMSNC and will submit it to the Central Political Conference for discussion after consulting with all parties. As for Chen's resignation, the Ministry of Communications believes that it will be able to overcome the difficulties.

Jin Li Yuan Wharf Case

Sandetang Appoints Arbitrator

Preliminary Exchange of Views Begins Yesterday

Regarding the Jin Li Yuan Wharf case of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, it is reported that the French Sandetang (a charitable organization) formally sent a letter to lawyer Gao Shuo yesterday, appointing an arbitrator to conduct arbitration. Yesterday afternoon, the two arbitrators had already begun discussions. The reporter from the "New Voice News" (新聲社) has learned the details of the matter and will report them as follows:

Sandetang Appoints Arbitrator Lawyer Ba He, representing Sandetang, has sent a letter to lawyer Gao Shuo, notifying him that Ya Mina has been appointed as the arbitrator. The original letter stated: "1. Sandetang has received your bureau's notification that lawyer Gao Shuo has been appointed as the arbitrator for the Jin Li Yuan Wharf case. Our office has also appointed Song Ya Mina as the arbitrator. Mr. Ya is residing at No. 25 Gongguan Road. The letter of appointment has been issued. Please check and liaise with him." It is reported that Ya Mina is currently the manager of the Jardine Matheson & Co.

Both Arbitrators Meet Yesterday After receiving the letter, lawyer Gao Shuo visited Ya Mina at around 3 PM yesterday to exchange views. According to Mr. Ya, he had prepared a written opinion on the arbitration and submitted it to the French Concession. He also requested lawyer Gao to prepare a written opinion to be submitted to the French Concession for adoption. Lawyer Gao Shuo immediately stated that the case had already departed from legal resolution and was proceeding with arbitration, so there was no need to prepare a written opinion for the French Concession. Mr. Ya said that this was solely for the sake of preserving the dignity of the French Concession and requested that it be followed. Lawyer Gao said that he would seriously consider this and requested that Mr. Ya first provide the written opinion for review. Mr. Ya scheduled to deliver it to Lawyer Gao this morning. The two discussed for over an hour.

Gao Shuo to Visit French Consul General Today Lawyer Gao Shuo visited the French Consul General yesterday afternoon but did not meet him. He is scheduled to visit again today to seek his opinion.

After the Lifting of the Ban on Hunan Rice

Large Quantities to Be Shipped to Shanghai

Various Shipping Companies Rush to Load

Hunan province is a rice-producing region. In the past, the amount of rice transported to Shanghai each year was very large. In recent years, due to poor harvests, the Hunan authorities banned the export of grain, and Hunan rice ceased to arrive in Shanghai. This year, there is a bumper harvest, and the Hunan authorities have lifted the ban on grain exports. Hunan rice, which has not been seen for several years, is once again being shipped to Shanghai. The First Batch of Hunan Rice Arrives in Shanghai After the Hunan army recovered the provincial capital, the residents were almost completely gone, and the government agencies were short of funds. The Provincial Government Committee decided that this year's Hunan province harvest is the best in over ten years. After providing for the province's own consumption, there is a surplus of rice that can be sold to other provinces. Therefore, it was decided to lift the ban, and the Hunan government will collect a certain amount of export permit fees per stone (unit of weight). After the decision, the grain merchants in Shanghai were notified and the first day of lifting the ban was August 22nd. Shanghai grain merchants have already telegraphed Hunan to place orders. The first batch to be shipped to Shanghai: yesterday, a local shipping company received information that over 1,000 bags have been shipped. The remaining large quantities will be loaded and shipped continuously.

Rushing to Send River Boats for Transport Hunan rice export brings a large transportation business opportunity. Upon hearing the news, various shipping companies in Shanghai are rushing to send ships to compete for loading. British Taikoo Dockyard Company has already dispatched four ships in the Changsha line, coordinating with Changjiang Shipping in Hankou to load this rice. Nissin Kisen Kaisha is also using four ships to carry the rice. On the Chinese side, Sanbei Shipping Company plans to send the Hongheng ship directly to Shanghai and Hunan, specifically to carry Hunan rice to Shanghai, and is also discussing it. China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will send the Liji ship, towing a large number of barges to Hankou, and then transshipping to Shanghai. It is expected that Hunan rice will arrive in Shanghai within the next week.

Jiangjing and Daji Collide on Tongzhou River

Both Ships Damaged and Sent to Shanghai for Repairs

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Changjiang River ship Jiangjing was sailing from Hankou to Shanghai. Yesterday morning at 5:30 AM, when it reached the Tongzhou river, it happened to encounter the Dada Company's Tongyang Line ship Daji, which had also weighed anchor from Tongzhou to Shanghai. At that time, Jiangjing was in front and Daji was behind, but the Daji suddenly accelerated, trying to overtake the Jiangjing. When the Daji was trying to overtake, the two ships became parallel, the Daji suddenly collided with the Jiangjing's front. The Jiangjing, seeing the fierce attack, attempted to evade it by accelerating forward, but it was too late. The bow of the Jiangjing was violently struck by the Daji, causing significant damage. The front of the Daji also suffered damage. Both ships immediately sailed to Shanghai, arriving at the port at 11 AM. Each reported to their headquarters and requested the customs river transport department to send personnel in the afternoon to inspect the losses of the two ships, investigate the faults of both parties, and determine a solution. The Jiangjing was originally scheduled to export today, but now needs to be repaired and its departure has been suspended. The Daji also needs to be repaired before it can sail.

Whereabouts of Prominent Figures

Zhu Lühe, Minister of Judicial Administration, left Beijing by express train at 5 PM yesterday and arrived in Shanghai at around 12 AM the same night.

Liu Jiwen, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, left Beijing by night train last night and is expected to arrive here around 7 AM this morning.

Increased Customs Fees

Additional Tax on Purchase of Clearance and Cargo Release Permits

Great Panic Among Shipping Companies

The customs recently received an order from the Inspector General of Customs that, starting from September 12th of this year, all requests for purchasing clearance and cargo release permits after 6 PM, on Sundays, and holidays, will be subject to an 80% increase in fees. Upon hearing the news, shipping companies in this port are in great panic, frowning and complaining. They have already reported to the Shipping Association, requesting that the authorities be urgently approached to negotiate and revoke the order to ease the burden. It is reported that the Shipping Association has separately presented the suffering of shipping merchants to the Ministry of Finance and the Inspector General of Customs, earnestly requesting the restoration of the original tax rate. It is unknown whether the authorities will revoke the order.

Flour Exports Have Not Yet Disappeared

The market price of flour has been rising sharply in recent days, and the Bureau of Social Affairs has issued an order for investigation. According to customs news yesterday, since the central government issued an order prohibiting flour exports to Tianjin, customs inspections have been very strict, and exports have virtually disappeared. However, greedy merchants are still secretly smuggling flour for export. The destination has been changed to Qingdao, Zhifu, Niuzhuang, Qinhuangdao, and other places for import. After landing, it is then transferred and sold to the Pingjin area (Beijing and Tianjin).

Wang Xiaolai Resigns

From the Position of Director of the Flour Special Tax Bureau

Since taking office, Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, has found his duties too numerous due to the complexity of chamber affairs and the need to constantly supervise and manage his private business. He found it difficult to juggle this with the duties as Director of the Flour Special Tax Bureau, and yesterday he specially telegraphed the Ministry of Finance to request his resignation. The original request stated: "Report on the election as Chairman of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, requesting approval to resign from the position. Since the National Government's revolutionary army pacified the southeastern provinces, Xiaolai has been repeatedly appointed to handle finance and reorganize taxation. For several years, I have been sincere and dedicated. I was then assigned by the Ministry to handle the collection of the Flour Special Tax in the Jiangsu-Zhejiang region. Implementing the plan, it has been two years. Everything that has happened should be clear. Considering that the Flour Special Tax was started in July of the seventeenth year [of the Republic, i.e. 1928], and ended in January of the eighteenth year, a total of seven months, a total of 1.1 million silver dollars were collected, an average of 150,700 silver dollars per month. Xiaolai took office as a tax collector, starting in February of the eighteenth year, and ending in July of this year, a total of eighteen months, collecting over 4 million silver dollars, averaging over 220,600 silver dollars per month. Comparing the tax revenue before and after, the amount has slightly increased, but this is not due to Xiaolai's abilities, but to the fact that the manufacturers understand the overall situation and work together to overcome difficulties. The Ministry takes into account the situation of merchants and protects production and transportation, and only then can there be this slight effect. Xiaolai dares not exaggerate his efforts, let alone rashly ask to leave. However, because Xiaolai is originally a merchant, engaging in the silk and tea industry, he was appointed as a committee member during the central government's reorganization of Shanghai merchant groups last year, and was later elected as a standing committee member. In June of this year, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce was formally established, and as a representative of the Silk Factory Guild, I was elected as an executive committee member, and also elected as a standing committee member. On July 1st, all committee members took office, and Xu Jizi was elected as Chairman in accordance with the law. However, Xu firmly resigned due to illness, and on August 20th, a temporary executive committee meeting was convened for re-election. Unexpectedly, after the election results were announced, Xiaolai was elected as Chairman. I immediately declared that I should consider it. Considering that the issue of the Chairman concerns the organization of the association, and a decision has been delayed, there is much suspicion. Xiaolai serves society with a long-held aspiration, and colleagues are urging, making it difficult to delay. If the organization cannot be sound due to personal advancement or retreat, especially at this time of tense situation, I am afraid that it will trigger unnecessary speculation and cause complications. However, the Chamber of Commerce is a legal organization for the public, and the Bureau is a national tax revenue agency. Xiaolai, holding both positions, fears that his talent is insufficient and his considerations may be inadequate. After much deliberation, I have no choice but to truthfully report to you, the Ministry Head, requesting your permission to resign from the position of Director of the Flour Special Tax Bureau in the Jiangsu-Zhejiang region, in order to avoid any delays. This is for the public good. I respectfully await your orders to comply."

Inland

Flour Mills Deny Inspection of Mill Wheat

The Inland Flour Mill Association held a meeting to oppose the Shanghai Agricultural Special Inspection Office of the Ministry of Agriculture and Mines establishing a branch in Jiangbei to inspect the wheat purchased by the flour mills. The news has been reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now heard that the Association has directly sent a letter to the Office, stating the reasons why it is difficult to implement. The original letter is recorded as follows: "To Director Jin of the Shanghai Agricultural Products Inspection Office of the Ministry of Agriculture and Mines, I am writing to you. We previously received your letter, along with five copies of the "Trial Measures for Inspecting Wheat in Various Counties of Jiangbei." Later, Deputy Director Jiang of your office delivered documents such as the "Circular Procedure" and instructed us to inform the factories and wheat farms in Jiangbei under our Association to report for inspection in accordance with the regulations. We immediately replied to Mr. Jiang that the inspection of wheat should not involve manufacturers, as this matter is of great importance to the future interests of inland factories. We would reply in writing after convening a meeting. Yesterday, our Association held a meeting and collectively discussed the matter. Everyone agreed that the inspection of wheat, in principle, is to improve the quality of agricultural products and prevent adulteration with water and fraud. It should be implemented on the farmers' side, following the methods of various countries around the world, inspecting the quality of agricultural products, determining grades, and strictly prohibiting fraud, so that there are no goods of poor quality or adulterated with water on the market. This is the fundamental solution. However, the inspection procedures stipulated by your office are not applied to farmers, but to manufacturers, which is neglecting the root and pursuing the branch, and is close to harassing the people. This should be revised. Also, the production of wheat in our country is the largest in the northern provinces, followed by Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, Anhui, Jiangsu, etc., and Shanghai is the largest market for wheat. The counties of Jiangbei are only the smallest area of wheat production in inland Jiangsu. Now, instead of opening offices in the important areas of various provinces at the same time, you are only setting up inspection offices in a corner of Jiangbei in Jiangsu, which not only cannot unify the methods, but also has partiality. This should be revised as well. Also, Article 4 of the Trial Measures states that the inspection of wheat will be carried out before transportation, export, import, and entry into the factory. Article 12 states that wheat that does not meet the standards may be ordered to be improved, or temporarily prohibited from transportation and sale, and may be given punishment according to the severity of the circumstances, with the penalty standard being up to three times the price of the goods, based on the weight of the water content and impurities exceeding the prescribed percentage. When manufacturers purchase wheat, at a time when the situation is stable and transportation is convenient, it is purchased from as far away as Shandong and Henan, and as close as Hubei and Anhui. Even at the present time, Hankou, Bengbu, and other places are purchasing areas. However, since there is no large agricultural product inspection office established in these provinces, the wheat purchased by the manufacturers has not been inspected. If it is transported to Jiangbei for import and your office inspects it and deems it unqualified, will you order it to be improved mid-way? The manufacturers are not willing to purchase this wheat of poor quality. If our factory does not purchase it, other factories will purchase it. Manufacturers take business needs as the purpose and cannot abandon the purchase because your office has not yet inspected it and needs to order the farmers to improve it. Now that it has been transported from a distant place, will you obstruct it at this time, or will you transport it back to the original place, order it to be improved, and then send it for inspection? Or will you temporarily prohibit transportation mid-way? If transportation is prohibited mid-way, the wheat will contain water and generate heat over time, and the flour milled out in the future will be of low quality, causing the manufacturers to suffer great losses. If you impose a penalty of three times the price of the goods according to your regulations, what crime have the manufacturers committed to suffer such trampling? This should be revised. Since the government has the grand aspiration of improving agricultural products, which common people would not be grateful for? The government should raise funds on its own, follow the good rules of various countries, and universally implement benevolent policies. Why take fees from the people and increase the burden on merchants? Moreover, since the government implemented the Flour Special Tax, the burden on our manufacturers has been heavy. Now, adding a wheat inspection fee of one cent per stone is tantamount to restoring wheat li [a type of tax], which is beyond our means. These are the main points. Other points, such as the inspection of wheat taking two or three hours, and the fact that staff must be sent to randomly sample and re-inspect wheat that has already been inspected, are either practically difficult to implement or prone to corruption during implementation, and are all difficult for our manufacturers to comply with. Therefore, we have specially written a letter detailing the reasons, respectfully hoping that you will examine and verify the matter. To Director Jin of the Shanghai Agricultural Products Inspection Office of the Ministry of Agriculture and Mines."
