Silk Cocoon Merchants Oppose the Import of Japanese Cocoons

Recently, due to the large-scale import of Japanese cocoons to Shanghai at low prices, resulting in fierce competition, the Chinese cocoon industry has been greatly affected. The cocoon merchants of various counties in Zhejiang Province specially telegraphed the National Government, requesting that it be banned or taxed heavily, in order to prohibit it through taxation. The original telegram reads: "To the Nanjing National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, and the Central Party Headquarters: Silk cocoons are a major product of Chinese farmers. Their sales to Europe and America are deeply and significantly related to the national economy and the people's livelihood. Recently, Japanese spring cocoons have been transported to China for sale at low prices, infringing on Chinese cocoons. It seems that there are already unscrupulous merchants colluding to purchase them in large quantities. If this situation is not prevented, they will continue to be transported to China, and our country's sericulture industry will be bankrupted. We urgently request that you strictly ban them and heavily tax the import of Japanese cocoons, prohibiting them through taxation, in order to maintain the industry. Zhejiang Province cocoon merchants (Jiaxing) Jiang Shifang, (Jiashan) Cheng Huilian, (Pinghu) Wang Weisan, (Haining) Zhong Guangyan, Wang Qingquan, (Shengxian) Lu Qinan, (Huzhou) Zhao Yi, etc. kowtow."

Temporary Meeting of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk Industry

Increase of 1.5 Fen Per Bolt of Silk Fabric Starting from November 1st

The Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk Weaving Joint Association held its 7th temporary meeting of the 5th session yesterday. Over 20 representatives from the Suzhou, Shengze, Danyang, and Shanghai silk industries attended. Wang Jie'an, the standing chairman, was elected as chairman, and Sun Zheng was elected as secretary. The ceremony was conducted in accordance with regulations. First, the chairman announced the purpose of convening the temporary meeting today. Then, after reading the documents and instructions from various departments of the National Government, the following resolutions were passed after public deliberation: (1) "Use Domestic Goods" proposal: Resolved to present a petition to the Training Department of the Central Government, ordering personnel of all levels of the party throughout the country to consistently follow the regulations and implement the use of domestic goods. Separately send telegrams to the provincial governments, requesting that they order the municipal and county governments to implement the issuance of proclamations and strictly urge all sectors to implement the use of domestic goods. (2) "Exemption of Silk Tax" proposal: Resolved to submit a petition again to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, requesting that after the implementation of the reduction of the likin tax, new taxes and levies should not be imposed on the moribund silk fabric industry under the pretext of compensation, in order to save it from ruin. (3) "Restriction of Cocoon Merchants" proposal: Resolved to telegram the Construction and Agriculture and Mines Departments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang Provinces again, requesting that they be executed in accordance with the proposal. (4) "Artificial Silk Factory" proposal: Resolved to retain it. (5) "Amendment of the Factory Law" proposal: Resolved to telegraph again to request amendment. (6) "Hiring a Permanent Legal Advisor for this Association" proposal: Resolved to retain it. (7) "Implementation of the New Price Scale" proposal: Resolved that the Association, in accordance with the public opinion of various Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, send a circular to the various trade associations, requesting that all goods comply with the resolution from September 11th to add 1.5 fen per bolt to the spring price scale, in order to protect the capital and save it from danger. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Citibank

Negotiations on the Dismissal of Chinese Employees

The Head Office Denies the Matter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

However, Tokyo and Yokohama Have Implemented the Policy

Regarding the case of Citibank dismissing Chinese employees in its various branches in Japan, it was previously reported by the Yokohama branch of the Kuomintang that the former Commercial Reorganization Association and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce had repeatedly sent personnel to negotiate with the bank. The bank replied that it was all rumors. However, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce continued to receive letters from the Yokohama Party branch, stating that the dismissal had already been implemented and that the bank had not fulfilled its promise to the Minister to give three months' salary and six months' obligation. Considering that this matter concerns the unemployment relief of overseas Chinese merchants, the Chamber passed a resolution at its seventh standing committee meeting to present it to the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs for verification. The letter is recorded below:

Letter from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to Citibank: "To Whom It May Concern: It was previously rumored that Citibank, with branches in Japan, was dismissing Chinese employees and replacing them with Japanese employees. The former Commercial Reorganization Association inquired with your bank and received a reply that it was not true. Now, on the 10th of this month, we received a letter from Yokohama, Japan, stating that the Tokyo branch of Citibank issued a notice on June 26th, dismissing all Chinese employees in July. The situation seems to be different from the previous rumors. Our Chamber cannot help but pay considerable attention to this matter. We are specially writing to your bank, hoping that you will investigate and show the truth. If what we have heard is true, can you help us mediate? Because among the customers of Citibank in Japan, the overseas Chinese in Japan should also account for the majority. In order to take care of the interests of Chinese customers and reconcile the feelings of all overseas Chinese, it is not appropriate to make too many changes. Moreover, at a time when the problem of unemployment is rampant in Japan, they are making every effort to exclude Chinese people. Your country's banks in Japan are purely in the position of a third party and should avoid this kind of disturbances."

Citibank's reply to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce: "Translation: We have received your letter and thank you for your concern about the dismissal of Chinese employees in our branches in Japan. However, as far as we know, the situation of Chinese employees in our branches in Japan has not changed since our previous contact with your Chamber. We hereby inform you of this."

Letter from the Yokohama Party branch to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce: "Regarding the incident of Citibank branches in Japan excluding Chinese employees, our department has repeatedly reported it to your Chamber and requested assistance, earnestly requesting a protest to the branch in Shanghai. Thanks to your enthusiasm and maintenance, and repeated negotiations with the head branch, the head branch has stated that it has no such malicious intention, and recently even stated that there has been no change. However, the various banks in Japan are cunning and intend to do so. As previously reported, the Tokyo branch implemented the dismissal of all Chinese employees at the end of June, and did not fulfill its obligation to the Minister to give a three-month advance notice and six months' salary (only paid three months). Recently, they have intensified their efforts and resorted to more sinister means to avoid the crime of excluding Chinese people. The matter is of great importance. We would like to inform you of their recent cunning plan. According to the investigation, the Tokyo branch of the bank issued a letter of recommendation to the dismissed Chinese employees, which did not specify the environmental reasons and stated that Japanese people must be used. In other words, it is necessary to be pro-Japanese and exclude Chinese people. Even a three-foot child can understand the fact that they are pro-Japanese and excluding Chinese people. This kind of letter of recommendation will not only put our Chinese employees in a desperate situation, but also give foreigners a guide to exclude Chinese people. Because our Chinese employees are now being excluded from the United States due to international relations, even if they want to transfer to other foreign banks, they will also be subject to the same excuse from other countries, and the Chinese are bound to be in a desperate situation. Moreover, if this trend starts, other foreign banks and companies may follow suit. If, unfortunately, the same thing happens again, tens of thousands of overseas Chinese will be in a desperate situation. It is heard that the various branches in Japan (such as Yokohama, Kobe, Osaka, Tokyo, etc.) know that we have filed a protest, so they have changed their cunning plan. For example, the Tokyo and Osaka branches have dismissed all Chinese employees, leaving only their compradors, not allowing them to leave, reducing their salaries, making their finances insufficient, changing their positions, making them appear unskilled, and unable to find a job again, so they have to resign automatically. Since they are resigning, the so-called six-month salary is hopeless. But if they reluctantly take the job, they have already intended to fire them, so why worry about them not being able to resign? Therefore, one can hide the evil of excluding Chinese people, and the other can save the six-month salary. Their intentions are insidious, comprehensive, and meticulous. At this moment, all the banks have put it into practice, and our Chinese employees have no place to stand. Therefore, we are specially writing to you and again urge your Chamber to protest, and be sure to expose their cunning plan, so that they cannot succeed, in order to maintain the livelihood of overseas Chinese in Japan. Otherwise, you must order all their branches in China, except for Americans, to use Chinese people, in order to conform to the practice of the branches in Japan. If not, then we can only send a telegram to the whole country, let everyone know their wickedness and resist trading with them, in order to show our resistance and extend justice. The matter concerns the survival of overseas Chinese. We hope that you will do your best to maintain it, and we will not give up until we achieve our goal. Before the letter, we are indignant and extremely expectant. Bao Yingzhang, Standing Committee Member of the Yokohama Direct Branch of the Kuomintang."

Reply from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to the Yokohama Party branch: "On the 20th of this month, we received your letter, stating that the Citibank branches in Japan dismissed Chinese employees, which has already been implemented, and attached two photographs of letters of recommendation, requesting us to protest again to maintain the livelihood of overseas Chinese in Japan. Regarding this matter, your letter said that the dismissal of all Chinese employees had been implemented at the end of June, and that the bank had not fulfilled its obligation to the Minister to give a three-month advance notice and six months' salary. This matter has already been negotiated by the Minister in Japan, and the so-called three-month advance notice and six-month salary indicate that the dismissal is a confirmed fact and cannot be reversed. However, your branch did not mention this in the previous letter, so the Shanghai head office was able to deal with it superficially and give empty promises. Now that the dismissal has been going on for two months, and the Minister and various groups in Japan have failed to negotiate successfully, it is difficult for our Chamber to reverse the situation afterwards. Therefore, after receiving your letter, our Chamber has passed a resolution at the standing committee meeting to present it to the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs for verification. We are now sending this letter in response to your request, and we will forward it to the Bureau of Social Affairs for joint verification. Please check it."

Local News 2

Record of the Fierce Battle Between Detectives and Bandits at the First Class Hotel

One Bandit Killed on the Spot

One Bandit Wounded and Captured

Chinese and Foreign Detectives Wounded by Gunfire

Commendable Courage in Capturing Thieves

Yesterday afternoon, at the Shanghai First Class Hotel at the intersection of Henan Road and Beijing Road, detectives and bandits exchanged gunfire during an arrest, resulting in a fierce shootout. As a result, one bandit was killed and another wounded. The wounded bandit was captured on the spot, and weapons were found in the room. Two detectives were wounded, one Western detective named Harvey and one Chinese detective named Wu Chunrong. The details are as follows:

Rushing to the Hotel: The Central Police Station on Fuzhou Road recently received a tip that several bandits were hiding in the Shanghai First Class Hotel at 229 Henan Road. Yesterday afternoon at approximately 3:50 PM, Western Inspector Luo Bingsheng, Western Detective Harvey, Platt, along with Chinese detectives Ding Huaguo, Sun Wen'an, Wu Chunrong, Tang Zengxiang, Ma Xiaozhi, Yin Shaochen, Ji Binkui, Pang Jinshan, and others, all armed, rushed to the aforementioned location. They learned that the bandits were staying in room 32 on the second floor. The detectives quietly ascended the stairs to make the arrest and stationed assistants at key points of entry and exit to prevent escape. Room 32 was located at the end of the corridor. As the detectives approached, the door was tightly closed, preventing them from seeing inside. Western Detective Harvey bravely kicked the door open, preparing to rush in. Detective and Bandit Exchange Gunfire: As soon as the door was kicked open, a bullet suddenly flew out of the room, hitting Harvey in the right arm before he could dodge. Harvey did not retreat and immediately returned fire. The bandits inside also fired continuously, resisting arrest. The Chinese and Western detectives fired back. The sound of gunfire echoed loudly, causing panic among the guests upstairs and downstairs. After about two or three minutes, the room fell silent. The detectives forced their way into the room and found a bandit lying stiffly on the ground, covered in blood. He was already dead. Another bandit, realizing that resistance was futile, surrendered.

Bandit Dead, Detectives Wounded: In this operation, in addition to Western Detective Harvey being wounded in the right arm, Chinese detective Wu Chunrong was also shot in the upper left chest. One bandit was killed and one wounded. The deceased had three gunshot wounds, all in vital areas. It was reported that a Chinese detective fired into the room from above through a gap in the ceiling, killing the bandit. The wounded bandit, named Chen Bingda, 25 years old, sustained two gunshot wounds to his legs and arms. He confessed that the deceased was Zheng Wanqing and admitted to being a thief. During the exchange, the detectives fired approximately 29 shots, while the bandits fired five or six. A set of smoking paraphernalia, a pistol, and six bullets were found in room 32. When the wounded bandit Chen Bingda was captured, the detectives ordered him to throw the pistol out of the room first before surrendering. Chinese detective Wu Chunrong was not aware of his injury at first. He hired a rickshaw to return to the police station. It was only when he undressed that he saw blood flowing profusely, realizing he had been wounded. The detectives' courage in arresting the bandits, disregarding their own safety, is commendable.

Impersonating Public Officials

Falsely Claiming to Be from the Garrison Headquarters

Extorting and Intimidating Officials and Civilians

The Bandits Have Been Questioned and Sentenced

To Be Handled by the Garrison Headquarters

Recently, Lu Sanjiu from Ningbo, Wei Songbai and Lu Qiaolin from Wuxi, Lu Fukun from Yancheng, and Lin Zijun and Chen Yangbing from Pudong, Shanghai, dared to falsely claim to be public officials of the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, extorting and intimidating people. They recently threatened Xie Renkun, Liu Fuyuan, and Xu Youfa, who resided at 3637 Zhoujiazui Road, extorting 1,000 yuan in cash. The case was discovered by Wang Bin, a detective of the Garrison Headquarters. He reported to Commander Xiong, who deemed their actions extremely illegal and ordered their immediate arrest and severe punishment. He immediately ordered the relevant department to prepare a document and dispatched the detective to the Hongkou Police Station to add detectives Feng Qi and Zhang Yuting to apprehend the suspects. Fortunately, the defrauded money was discovered early and had not yet been divided up and spent. All the money was recovered, and counterfeit epaulettes were confiscated. Additional Women's Organizations

Women Police Movement

Preparing for a Large-Scale Promotion

According to the Continental Daily, women's organizations in Shanghai, in view of the current social situation in Shanghai, believe that there is an increasing need to establish women police. They are currently preparing for a large-scale promotional campaign as a preliminary step. After investigating the situation of female workers, the committee suggested that the most effective way to deal with the various adverse environments is for the Municipal Council to organize a female police squad, granting them all the powers of patrolmen to supervise dance halls and factories, strictly implement health programs, and arrest criminal offenders. Because women are better able to understand women's issues, this female patrol is bound to be immensely useful in all social welfare work. Currently, many major cities around the world have added women police, with remarkable results. If Shanghai can follow suit, it will surely lead to a rapid solution to most of the problems that women who are concerned about social conditions are usually anxious about. However, according to the leaders of women's organizations, when the plan was first solicited for opinions from the Municipal Council and the police station, few people agreed. But it is expected that after public promotion, the authorities will give it a try.

French Concession

Strictly Prohibiting Flower Gambling Houses

Seven Flower Gambling Houses Raided

Lin Asi Fined 3,000 Yuan

Gamblers Also Questioned and Fined Separately

The French Police Department has been strictly prohibiting flower gambling in the concession, and a special gambling arrest squad was formed, managed by Detectives Li Yousheng and Li Liansheng, and Plainclothes Detective Liu Kunbao. Recently, a large number of flower gambling houses were raided, including the flower gambling headquarters set up by Lin Asi at 18 Pushi Lane, Pushi Road, employing Shen Xinglin, Chen Ayuan, Gu Changsheng, Wang Asan, and Shi Guangzu as accomplices; Wang Xiaoji at 48 Yuzhen Street outside Xiaodongmen; Zeng Renshan at 21 of the same street; Wang Aer at 32 Baxianfang, Baxian Bridge, employing Chen Rongqing, Tan Amao, and Zhang Jinshan as accomplices; gamblers Gong Furen, Wang Yiru, Gao Xinhe, Wang Jinrong; Pang Amao at 4 Dapu Bridge; Zhu Xuzhong at 435 Jin Shenfu Road, running a flower gambling house, gamblers Zhang Shusheng, Yang Wuyou, Jiang Dayuan, accomplices Wu Zhongsheng, Yu Bingrong, Lu Youcai, Zhang Yushun, Gu Xirong, Yang Shengui, Gong Xibing, Ruan Liuyi, Gong Ashun; Wang Axiang's flower gambling listening post at 1 Yude Lane, Malan Road, gamblers Shen Zhaofu, Xie Qidong, Qian Jinsheng, Ji Aer, Tang Gensheng, Zhang Yonggen, women Wang Zhoushi, Mei Jishi, Shen Lishi, and others, a total of seven places. A large number of flower gambling evidence and gambling money were confiscated and taken to the police station. Yesterday, they were sent to the French Concession Court for investigation. Western Detective Powerdi first reported the situation, stating that the defendants' private flower gambling was harmful to society. The defendants all admitted to setting up private flower gambling houses. The Chinese and Western judge sentenced Lin Asi to a fine of 3,000 yuan, or two years in prison; Wang Xiaoji and Zeng Renshan to a fine of 1,500 yuan each, or one year in prison; Wang Aer, Gong Amao, Zhu Xuzhong, and Wang Axiang to a fine of 1,000 yuan each, or one year in prison; Shen Xinglin, Chen Ayuan, Wang Asan, Shi Guangzu, Chen Rongqing, Tan Amao, and Chen Jinshan to a fine of 200 yuan each, or six months in prison; Gu Changsheng was not supposed to leave the country and return, and was sentenced to one month for violating the law, and fined 200 yuan. If unable to pay the fine, he will be imprisoned for six months; Gong Furen, Wang Yiru, Gao Xinhe, Wang Jinrong, Zhang Shusheng, Yang Wuyou, Jiang Dayuan, Wu Zhongsheng, Yu Bingrong, Lu Youcai, Zhang Yushun, Gu Xirong, Yang Shengui, Gong Xibing, Ruan Liuyi, Gong Ashun, Shen Zhaofu, Xie Qirong, Qian Jinsheng, Jin Hongsheng, Ji Aer, Tang Gensheng, Wu Agen, Zhang Yonggen, and other 24 people, were fined 50 yuan each, or six weeks in prison; women Wang Zhoushi, Mei Lishi, and Shen Lishi were fined 20 yuan each, or two weeks in prison as a warning. The seized gambling evidence and silver dollars were all confiscated.

Englishman Accuses Wife of Adultery

Pregnant After Adultery with a Greek Man

Witnesses Testify to Having Seen It

Lance, a 54-year-old Englishman and manager of a foreign firm at 47 Beijing Road, recently hired a lawyer to file a criminal complaint in the Special District Court against Greek man McLeay for disrupting his family, having an affair with his wife, and inciting her to flee. The court approved the request and summoned McLeay to the Second Criminal Court yesterday morning. The plaintiff Lance stated that he married Ms. Washington in Kobe, Japan, in 1917, and they had children. In 1925, his wife and children came to Shanghai to study and lived at 71 Doulean Road, while he went to Tianjin for business. He recently returned to Shanghai and learned that his wife had an affair with the defendant, but he did not witness it. On the evening of July 1, he received a report from his friend Liddell, who said that he saw his wife alone at apartment number 1, 24 Kunshan Road, the afternoon before, and that she did not leave until the next morning. After further investigation, he learned that the place was the defendant's residence and that his wife was currently pregnant with the defendant's child. All his decorations and furniture were taken by the defendant. He requested an investigation. The defendant stated that he was an engineer and resided at 192 Yuyuan Road. Regarding the plaintiff's accusations, (1) he claimed that as for the adultery with his wife, the plaintiff's wife is also in court and can testify. (2) As for the items that were taken, those items were originally his. Lance's wife also filed a statement admitting that she did visit the defendant at 24 Kunshan Road and had an affair with him, claiming that she committed adultery under the instructions of her husband. After reviewing the statements, Judge Sun Yuan ordered that the case be rescheduled for further hearing.

One Punch Kills a Man

Conflict Over Food

Gu Linzhen Dies After Being Punched

Gu Linzhen, a 43-year-old man from Jiangyin, worked at the Meida Tofu Shop owned by Xie Jintao at 618 Datong Road, Zhabei. While having dinner the night before, he went outside to relieve himself due to sudden urgency. When he returned, half of his share of food had disappeared (the shop provided three meals a day, with each worker having one bowl of vegetables to eat separately). He then discovered that his colleague Jiang Honggao from Hangzhou had stolen it, so he loudly berated Jiang, grabbing him to argue. However, Jiang swore that he did not steal his vegetables. They disagreed and started fighting. Gu had hemoptysis, making him physically weak. Jiang was only 19, but he was very strong. He punched Gu in the waist, causing Gu to fall to the ground without moving. At first, they thought he was pretending, but he did not get up for a long time. When they touched him, his body was cold as ice, and he had already died. Xie Jintao, the shop owner, knew that Jiang had caused trouble and was afraid of being implicated, so she called Zheng (39 years old), the deceased's wife from Changzhou, and together with Hu Qianyin, the watchman of the area, they took Jiang to the Fourth District Headquarters. Director Jin conducted a preliminary investigation and found that Jiang had killed a man with one punch, which was a strange occurrence. Fearing that the deceased might have had underlying health issues, he ordered the local headman to report to the court for an autopsy. Yesterday afternoon, Inspector Xu conducted the autopsy and found that Gu Linzhen had indeed died from being hit in the waist. The family was ordered to prepare the coffin, and the murderer Jiang Honggao was taken to the judicial department for investigation.

Confession in the Parricide Case (Continued) (Yesterday)

Sun Liansheng Admits to the Murder

The Case is Now Completely Clear

The confession of Sun Liansheng, who killed his adoptive father Sun Laowu, was not fully recorded yesterday. The following is a continuation:

Sun Fusheng: Official (Question) Testimony of Sun Fusheng, 39 years old, residing at 6 Hengxin Lane, Wai Ma Road, working as a driver. The deceased Sun Laowu was my fifth uncle. I am from the eldest branch of the family. Sun Liansheng is from the third branch and was adopted by Sun Laowu for two or three years. (Question) How was his behavior usually? (Answer) Greedy and lazy. Two days before my fifth uncle died, he told me that Liansheng had stolen money the first time, and sold the car the second time. Liansheng wanted to kill him and asked me to write a letter to the countryside, asking Liansheng's father to come. I asked the accountant to write the letter. It was a case of a son wanting to kill his father, and a father wanting to kill his son, so I asked Liansheng's father to come to Shanghai quickly. However, the letter did not arrive before he died. I learned about my fifth uncle's death on the third day. The neighbor of the deceased, Chen Guanghua, sent a letter to my cousin Jiang Yinsheng, who relayed it to me. I first sent a telegram and then went to Jiangwan. I saw the deceased on the ground, half of his face was gone, and only half of his neck was connected. He was shirtless and only wearing a pair of pants. Three of his left fingers were broken. The prosecutor came to perform the autopsy at 3:00 PM. (Question) What was the name of the ship to Tianshenggang? The answer was either Dada or Datong, but it always departed around 1:00 AM. After Liansheng was captured, at my father Sun Xueli and his father Sun Xuewen's place, he admitted to murdering his fifth uncle. Qiu Lansheng was captured on the third day because the neighbor said that Ji Shuangquan was staying at his house, so he ordered Qiu to lead the capture. Ji Shuangquan ran away and eventually went to the deceased's house, pretending to inquire, so he was captured. (Question) How did you know that Ji Shuangquan was the murderer? (Answer) Before the deceased died, he often told the neighbors that they wanted to change his mind and asked the neighbors to visit his house often. (Question) How did the neighbors not know when Sun Laowu was killed? (Answer) The so-called neighbors lived far away. The nearest neighbor was a Cantonese family who were merchants and had no contact with them on a regular basis.

Sun Xuewen: Official (Question) Testimony of Sun Xuewen, 60 years old, from Shatou Town, Tongzhou. Sun Liansheng is my son and has been adopted by Sun Laowu as his son. On the third day, Liansheng and Qiu Shuntao were arrested at my nephew's house in Tongzhou. (Question) How did your brother Sun Laowu die? Did you ask your son? (Answer) At first, he refused to say, but later on the ship, he admitted that Ji Shuangquan used a knife, Qiu Shuntao used a hoe, and Liansheng used scissors, and Qiu Lansheng used a shovel to kill him. He told me that himself.

Sun Xueli: Official (Question) Testimony of Sun Xueli, 65 years old. Liansheng is my nephew. He said on the ship that Qiu Shuntao was the middleman for selling the car for 50 yuan, and he had already received the money. Because he did not have a permit, and Sun Laowu refused to take out the permit, the Shandong man who bought the car returned the car, and Liansheng had to return the money. While Liansheng was in the Fifth District Bureau in the jail, I asked him how Laowu died. He said that Ji Shuangquan took the knife, Qiu Shuntao took the hoe, and Qiu Lansheng took the shovel, and he himself took the scissors. (Question) When you asked him, did you ask if they had discussed it before killing Laowu? (Answer) Of course, they discussed it together.

Sun Faming: Official (Question) Testimony of Sun Faming, 40 years old, from Tongzhou, in the automobile business. Sun Liansheng is my cousin. On the morning of the third day of the intercalary June, at 9:30 AM, I received a telegram saying that Sun Laowu had died. Around 10:00 AM, I was not at home. My wife was washing rice outside the door. Liansheng and Qiu Shuntao passed by. My wife asked them where they came from. They said they came from Shanghai. My wife insisted on keeping them for lunch and went outside to discuss it with others. Then they tied up Liansheng and Shuntao. When I returned home in the afternoon, I questioned him. At first, he said that Laowu was not dead, but later he said that Ji Shuangquan and others had killed him. They had discussed it three months ago. (Question) Did you ask Qiu Shuntao? (Answer) He refused to speak, and we did not ask him. But during the interrogation in the Fifth District, they mostly admitted to it.

Chen Guanghua: Official (Question) Testimony of witness Chen Guanghua, 42 years old, from Nantong, living in the Jiangwan Racecourse, making a living by farming. He was a close friend of Sun Laowu, whose house was three li away. He came to my house at 5:30 AM on the first day and said that Liansheng wanted to harm him. I told him to tell Sun Fusheng, and he taught me to go and watch the house. On the morning of the third day, at 6:00 AM, the carpenter Jiang came to report the news, and only then did I know that the reason was the sale of the rickshaw, which Laowu did not allow.

Xu Farong: Official (Question) Testimony of Xu Farong, 58 years old, from Nantong, living in Jiangwan. Sun Laowu is my cousin. I don't know how he died. On the third day, Chen Guanghua came to report the news, and only then did I know. I don't know who killed him.

Wu Xiqi: Official (Question) Testimony of Wu Xiqi, 31 years old, from Nantong, living in Jiangwan, making a living by farming. I don't know Sun Laowu. Ji Shuangquan helped me farm for one day. (Question) Did he come to your house on the night of the second day? (Answer) Yes, he did. (Question) When? (Answer) At 10:00 PM. He said he came to avoid the rain and slept there. He left at dawn. (Question) Were there any blood stains? (Answer) He came at night and left before dawn, so it was hard to tell in the dark.

Wang Da: Official (Question) Testimony of Wang Da, 37 years old, from Rugao, living in Zhangjiazhai, Qujiaqiao, making a living by farming. Sun Laowu was my friend. (Question) Did you know about the matter of their uncle and nephew selling the car? (Answer) I knew. His nephew had already sold the car, and Sun Laowu went to get it back. He went to Shanghai on the first day. At 7:00 PM, I went to his house to chat and left at 9:00 PM. Sun Liansheng did not enter the Du gate because of the car matter. Later, I went out and saw Ji Shuangquan and Qiu Shuntao on the street, along with two people I did not recognize. I asked them where they were going, and they said they were going to play.

Jiang Jiashun: Official (Question) Testimony of Jiang Jiashun, 41 years old, from Tongzhou, living in Jiangwan, working as a carpenter. (Question) Did Qiu Lansheng eat snails with you on the second day? (Answer) No. (Question) Did Ji Shuangquan give Qiu Lansheng two catties of snails? Do you know about this? (Answer) I don't know. I went to Xu Farong's house with my family on the second day.

At this point, the official summoned all the defendants to the court to confront the witnesses. Sun Liansheng initially tried to deny it, but his father, Sun Xuewen, said, "You told me very clearly. If you intended to kill your uncle, it would be worth it to pay with your life. If it was someone else's intention, just say it and don't take the blame for others." At this point, Sun Liansheng claimed that Ji Shuangquan had acted first, Qiu Shuntao had dragged the uncle off the bed, and he had taken the scissors. The official asked, "Did you stab him?" (Answer) "No, I didn't stab him." The official asked, "If you didn't do it, would others dare to do it?" (Answer) "I was the fourth one to do it, and I made a cut on his foot with the knife." (Question) "You were the second one to stab him in the neck." Sun Liansheng hesitated in response. The official asked, "How many days did you discuss it?" (Answer) "On the first day, at the Luo Jinmiao Bridge, Liu Junchuan, Wei Qiaohai, Ji Shuangquan, Qiu Lansheng, and Qiu Shuntao sat on the stone and discussed it." The official said, "Don't accuse anyone wrongly." (Answer) "That's the truth." Thus, the case was completely cleared up.

Municipal Public Safety Bureau

Shutting Down Ankangli's Artesian Well

Deadline to Switch to Tap Water

Compulsory Enforcement If Violated

There are 53 buildings with approximately 100 households in Ankangli, Yongxing Road, Zhabei. An artesian well was originally installed and registered with the Municipal Public Works Bureau at the end of November of the eighteenth year. At that time, the water volume was sufficient, and residents had no complaints. Unexpectedly, at the beginning of this month, the well suddenly ran out of water, causing panic among the residents. The case was reported through the Party Department and forwarded to the Public Works Bureau for handling. The bureau sent staff to investigate and found that the well was being overused due to the summer heat, causing the well to be clogged with fine sand, thus hindering the water flow. The water level in the water tower was almost non-existent. The owner was hiring workers to dredge the well and open the public taps in the neighborhood to provide water. However, the well's pump was a Wellington No. 2, which required at least a 5-horsepower motor. The current motor only had 3 horsepower. It could barely be used for a new well, but the well was old, the water source was low, and the water tower was high, resulting in insufficient power. The Public Works Bureau sent a letter to Ankang Real Estate Company, the owner, ordering them to replace the motor with a 7.5-horsepower motor. If the repair work would take more than three days, tap water should be connected first to ensure the water supply for the residents. However, after more than ten days, the owner had not complied. Yesterday, the bureau sent another warning letter, setting a deadline of three days to completely switch to tap water. Failure to comply would result in compulsory enforcement in accordance with the city's water supply regulations.

Large-Scale Reconstruction of Houses in Minhang Town

City Appearance Renewed

The houses along Xianglidao and Zhangjialong South in Minhang Town were severely damaged and presented a dangerous situation. District Chief Wu sent letters to the house owners, inviting them to discuss reconstruction, obtain construction permits, and comply with the resolutions of the first county administrative conference, requiring the main streets to be no less than 5 meters wide and the alleyways to be no less than 2 meters wide. The streets and lanes were widened in accordance with the regulations. A large portion has already been completed, and the city appearance has been renewed. The reconstruction of houses in the area south of Danong and the old West Street is also under discussion and actively underway.

Announcement by the Municipal Public Safety Bureau

Simplified Chart of Population Changes

Yuan Liang, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Public Safety Bureau, in order to rectify the population census, eliminate hidden dangers, and maintain public order, has specially drawn up a simplified chart of population changes and ordered painters to paint it in prominent places in Zhabei and Huxi, so that merchants and people in all places can be impressed and implement it. The chart is divided into eight items: birth, entry, death, emigration, immigration, adoption, relocation, inheritance, and marriage. If any of the above items occur, they should be reported to the police station in charge. Failure to report any of the above matters will result in detention for up to ten days or a fine of up to ten yuan upon discovery. If the report is not truthful when staff members conduct a spot check, detention for five to thirty days or a fine of five to thirty yuan will be imposed if inconsistencies are discovered later.

Ge Yuming Sentenced for Adultery

Sentenced to Three Months in Prison

Ge Yuming was accused of adultery with Wei Suqin, the wife of Cheng Youren, an employee of the Zhonghua Book Company. His superiors dismissed him for tarnishing official ethics. However, the initial trial of the lawsuit resulted in Ge's victory. Cheng was unwilling to accept the result and filed an appeal against Ge and Wei. Wei had already left Shanghai, and the appeal hearing did not appear. Cheng went to the countryside to find the former maid A Qiao to testify to the adultery. Judge Zhou of the Special District Court decided to postpone the verdict on Wei's part and hold another hearing. The debate on Ge's part has ended, and the judgment was rendered yesterday afternoon. The appellant's lawyers, Xue Jiaqi and Wu Chengyu, were present in court to await the verdict. The court revoked the original judgment that Ge Yuming was not guilty of adultery. Ge Yuming was sentenced to three months of imprisonment for adultery with Wei Suqin. However, Ge expressed dissatisfaction in court and requested permission to appeal.

Lost Boy Waiting to be Claimed

Yesterday, the Municipal Public Security Bureau received a lost boy, Tian Daidai (aka Xu Daidai), from the Third Precinct of the Sixth District. According to him, he is thirteen years old, from Lan Ni Du, Pu Dong, and has a mother and older sister at home. His mother knits foreign socks, his sister [blank space], and his father, Xu Baoming, was a carpenter who passed away many years ago. [Blank space] went out to play and got lost because he did not know the way. The boy has a shaved head, wears a broken light blue cloth jacket and dark blue cloth trousers, and is barefoot without shoes or socks. The child was instructed to be handed over to the Third Precinct for investigation of his family, but to no avail. He has now been sent to the Women and Children Relief Association for care and to await being claimed.

Shanghai Bank Jing'an Temple Road Branch New Commencement

The Jing'an Temple Road Branch of Shanghai Bank has recently expanded its premises to provide even more thorough service. In light of the rapid rise and fall of silver prices, local merchants are eager to be informed in advance. Therefore, every morning at 8:00 AM, the branch will hang up a large price chart in front of its door, so that merchants living in the area can know the trend of silver prices before going to their companies. Furthermore, as there are many shops in the area engaged in import and export, the branch will also handle foreign exchange business for the convenience of customers, such as foreign exchange mortgage, drafts, letters of credit, traveler's checks, and buying and selling gold coins of various countries, etc.

Temporary Clinic of the Banking Association Closes

The Banking Association established a temporary hospital in the Banking Guild Hall on North Henan Road last month. As there have been fewer severe epidemic cases this summer compared to previous years, and few people have sought treatment at the hospital in the more than forty days since it opened, it seems unnecessary to continue operating the hospital now that it is autumn and fewer people are seeking treatment. Yesterday, the committee decided to close the clinic from yesterday onwards.

Various Ports Come to Shanghai to Hire Female Hairdressing Technicians

Zhang Zizhen, manager of Nanyang Java Commercial Co., Ltd., arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday and went to the Shanghai Women's Hairdressing School on West Gate Road to hire technicians Jiang Ziqiang, Yang Guifu, Bai Zongqing, Chen Siying, Wang Yufeng, and Xu Guiying. They are currently processing their passports and awaiting their departure by ship. Anqing, Huai'an, and Zhenjiang have also sent letters to the school requesting three or four technicians each. The school has already made appropriate selections and they will depart soon. Currently, the school, seeing that there is a great demand for technicians in various places, plans to expand the number of students and recruit many new students from August 15th.

He Qingzeng Organizes Heji Cosmetic Company

After returning to China from studying in the United States, He Qingzeng organized Heji Cosmetic Manufacturing Company, with an office located in the Hechang Foreign Firm at 7 Ningbo Road. He selected the most needed ordinary fragrances from China's cosmetic and soap making industries and combined them into various types. The prices are much lower than imported goods, and the quality is even better.

Investigating the Origin of Sixty-One Yuan Banknotes

At 6:40 AM yesterday morning at the Shanghai South Railway Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, as the station was preparing the second early express train to Hangzhou, a boy of about fourteen or fifteen years old came to the station to buy a ticket to Hangzhou. While the boy was wandering around the ticket office, a man of about twenty years old pointed to the boy and told the police that the boy was carrying a roll of banknotes that he had pickpocketed on a tram, so he followed him to the station. The police interrogated the boy, who said his name was Chen Jinquan, fifteen years old, from Hangzhou. He came to Shanghai from Hangzhou in April to find his older brother Zhong Changsheng, who now runs a "Swallow's Nest" in the Shunxing Building on Dongxin Bridge in the French Concession. His brother is his father's son by a previous marriage, so their surnames are different. The sixty-one yuan in banknotes were stolen from his brother last night while he was asleep because his brother and sister-in-law often beat and scolded him. He did not pickpocket it on a tram. The police took both parties to the chief of police at the South Station. Chief Lou interrogated them and their statements were the same. The police were sent to investigate the Shunxing Building on Dongxin Bridge in the French Concession and asked his brother Zhong Changsheng to come forward. Together with the person and the money, they were bailed out.

Letter

To the Editor, We read in your newspaper on August 22nd, in the local news column, a section about an apprentice being electrocuted to death. The Xing Yu Xing printing company rented a portion of a downstairs unit from our company; the deceased, Weng Dingfang, was an apprentice of the printer. The fan, where the incident took place, was installed out of the way, in a corner. The apprentice was an employee of the evening shift, and was, during the evening break, standing, playing in an otherwise unused spot, when he stepped on the electrical wiring, which led to his death. The story published by your paper has some differences from the facts. We therefore request that the letter be published in the letter section for correction. Sincerely, Wenhua Fine Arts Books and Printing Company.

Educational News Highlights

Ministry of Education to Reorganize Private Universities and Vocational Schools

Plans to Formulate Reward and Ban Measures

(Central News Agency) The Ministry of Education has recently been actively planning to reorganize private universities, colleges, and vocational schools across the country. The measures for rewarding and banning private universities, colleges, and vocational schools have now been formulated and are described as follows:

Reward Measures: (1) Private universities, colleges, and vocational schools that have been registered and have excellent performance may be subsidized by the central or provincial governments, or the Ministry of Education may transfer funds from the Education Fund Committee to provide subsidies. (2) Colleges or departments that have made special contributions to education and academics may be commended by the Ministry of Education or provincial and municipal education administrative organs, or be given subsidies. (3) Those with an experimental nature and excellent experimental results may be commended by the Ministry of Education or given subsidies.

Banning Measures: (1) Private universities, colleges, and vocational schools that have not been registered shall be ordered to apply for registration within a specified period of time. Those who fail to apply for registration as scheduled shall be ordered to suspend operations. Those who apply for registration in compliance with the order shall be inspected and approved for registration, or approved for trial operation, or ordered to suspend operations, or ordered to end operations within a specified period of time, or immediately closed down. (2) Private universities, colleges, and vocational schools that have been registered shall be inspected by the Ministry of Education at any time. If the content does not meet the prescribed standards, or if the deficit is too large, the Ministry of Education shall, depending on the circumstances, order them to improve within a specified period of time, or prepare for violations, or give warnings or close them down. Those who fail to improve after being guided by the Ministry of Education shall be warned. If the situation is serious, or if they fail to improve after a certain period of time after being warned, they will be closed down. (3) Newly established private universities, colleges, and vocational schools shall be operated in accordance with the laws and regulations of universities and vocational schools, and shall first apply for establishment in accordance with the private school regulations. Those who are arrested will be immediately closed down.

Eighteenth Year of Jiangsu Counties

Summary of Statistical Overview of Compulsory Education

The Jiangsu Provincial Compulsory Education Joint Preparatory Office recently compiled statistics on the general situation of compulsory education in Jiangsu counties in the current year (18th year). The main points are extracted below.

(1) The total number of schools this year is 8,284. There are more than 300 schools in Yancheng, Wujin, Nantong, and Wuxi counties. There are more than 200 schools in Jiangyin, Nanhui, Rugao, Yixing, Songjiang, and Funing counties. There are less than 100 schools in 24 counties, and there are less than 40 schools in Siyang, Lishui, Ganyu, Yangzhou, and Donghai counties. (2) The total number of grades is 13,825, with the most being 760 grades in Wujin, followed by 635 grades in Wuxi, and the least being 31 grades in Yangzhou, followed by 35 grades in Donghai. The difference between counties is huge, and the ratio of the number of schools to the number of grades is not the same. (3) The total number of teachers is 19,637. Only Wujin has more than 1,000 teachers. There are less than 100 teachers in Lishui, Jiangpu, Yangzhou, Yizheng, Donghai, and Ganyu counties. The difference between 28 teachers in Donghai and 1,123 teachers in Wujin is more than 40 times. (4) The total number of children is 547,103. There are more than 10,000 people in Wujin etc. (30193-10094) in 17 counties, and more than 1,000 people in Liyang etc. (9744-1138) in 43 counties. Only Donghai has less than 1,000 people (847). (5) The total amount of funding is 4,445,671 yuan. More than 100,000 yuan is found in Suzhou City and Wuxi etc. (255848, 24517-107052) in 16 counties. The remaining 45 counties have more than 10,000 yuan (Nanhui 99729 Yangzhou 10236). (6) According to the total number of the above items, the average number of grades per school is 1.67, the number of teachers is 2.37, the number of children is 660.4, and the funding required is 356.77 yuan. Also, the average number of children per grade is 39.57, the number of teachers required is 1.23, and the funding required is 321.63 yuan. (In the previous year, the average number of children per grade was 37.57, the number of teachers was 1.44, and the funding required was 306.34 yuan.) Also, each teacher educates an average of 27.86 children, and each child spends 8.13 yuan per year. (In the previous year, each teacher educated an average of 26.17 children, and each child accounted for 8.15 yuan in county fees.) In terms of the value of educational economics, this year is more advanced than the previous year. (7) The total number of items this year is higher than the previous year, but the increase or decrease varies greatly when comparing counties and cities. The number of schools increased in 37 counties, and decreased in 24 counties and 1 city. The number of grades increased in 40 counties and 1 city, and decreased in 20 counties. The number of teachers increased in 42 counties and 1 city, and decreased in 19 counties. The number of children increased in 50 counties and 1 city, and decreased in 11 counties. The amount of funding increased in 44 counties and 1 city, and decreased in 17 counties. There are no counties or cities that have maintained the status quo. (8) Compared with the previous year, the total number of increases is less than the previous year, which shows that the proportion of increase this year is less than the proportion of increase in the previous year. For example, the increase in funding in the previous year was 907,214 yuan, while this year it was only 307,245 yuan. Also, the increase in children in the previous year was 42,657, while this year it was only 39,459. (9) This year, the total number of private schools has decreased compared with the previous year. The number of schools has decreased by 80, the number of grades has decreased by 118, the number of teachers has decreased by 4, and the number of children has decreased by 2,182. However, the funding has increased by 11,780 yuan, but in terms of educational efficiency, it has decreased. (10) This statistics is based on the statistical tables of primary schools and primary departments of primary schools filled out by the education bureaus of 61 counties in Jiangsu and the Suzhou Municipal Government. In order to understand the general situation of four-year compulsory education in 61 counties in Jiangsu and Suzhou City in the 18th year, and to compare it with the 17th year to see the growth and decline of compulsory education, the Jiangsu Provincial Education Department ordered the issuance.

Temporary Measures for Registration and Examination of Private School Teachers

The Jiangsu Education Department issued an order to the Education Bureau to implement the "Temporary Measures for Registration and Examination of Private School Teachers" and three types of forms in various counties of Jiangsu Province, and to report on their implementation. The order stated: The Education Department previously promulgated Article 7 of the "Provisional Regulations for the Administration of Private Schools in Jiangsu Province," which stipulates the format of the "Application for Establishing a Private School" and the "Permit for Establishing a Private School" should be formulated by the Education Department. Furthermore, Article 18 of the same regulations, the measures for registration and examination of private school teachers, should also be formulated by the Education Department. Now, eleven articles of the "Temporary Measures for Registration and Examination of Private School Teachers in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province," the "Application for Establishing a Private School in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province," the "Permit for Establishing a Private School in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province," and the "Registration Form for Private School Teachers in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province" are hereby formulated and issued, ordering the bureau director to follow the regulations, actively implement them, and report on the implementation. This order.

Article 1 of the "Temporary Measures for Registration and Examination of Private School Teachers in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province" is formulated in accordance with Article 18 of the "Provisional Regulations for the Administration of Private Schools in Jiangsu Province." Article 2: All private school teachers in various counties must fill out two copies of the prescribed private school teacher registration form and submit them to the Education Bureau of each county for registration. The aforementioned private school teacher registration form will be specified separately. Article 3: After registration, all private school teachers in various counties must undergo examination, which is divided into two types: examination with testing and examination without testing. Article 4: Private school teachers in various counties who possess one of the following qualifications may undergo examination with testing: A. Graduates of higher elementary schools or secondary vocational schools; B. Students who have studied in junior middle schools for two or more years; C. Those who have served as elementary school teachers for one or more years; D. Those who have taught in private schools for three or more years and have a thorough understanding of the meaning of texts. Article 5: Private school teachers in various counties who possess one of the following qualifications may undergo examination without testing: A. Graduates of simplified normal schools or normal training institutes for two or more years; B. Graduates of middle schools or higher; C. Elementary school teachers who have passed the examination and whose validity period has not expired; D. Those who have served as elementary school teachers for three or more years and have excellent performance, with comments from the county supervisor or education committee member. Article 6: The subjects for the private school teacher examination with testing are as follows: A. (Party Principles) The Three Principles of the People; B. (National Language) Understanding phonetic symbols, proficiency in modern punctuation, and ability to write coherent text; C. (Arithmetic) Abacus or written calculation, able to solve four operations and simple equations; D. (General Knowledge) Natural, social, and hygiene knowledge; E. (Oral Examination) Correct pronunciation, coherent language; F. (Physical Fitness) No hidden diseases. Article 7: Private school teachers who pass the examination with testing or are qualified for examination without testing may be issued a private school teacher permit by the county Education Bureau, with a provisional validity period of three years. However, those who meet the qualifications for examination without testing must first obtain various supporting documents from the private school teacher and submit them to the county Education Bureau director for strict review before being issued. Article 8: Those who do not have a private school teacher permit should be strictly investigated and prohibited from being private school teachers by the county Education Bureau. Those who have already established private schools will have their private schools closed. Article 9: The private school teacher examination with testing will be held once a year, with the time determined by each county. The county Education Bureau will compile a report of the qualified private school teachers at the end of the year and submit it to the Education Department for record. Article 10: If a qualified private school teacher violates any of the following conditions, the county Education Bureau may revoke their permit and close their private school: A. Violating the principles of the Kuomintang; B. Not meeting the standards for establishing a private school; C. Disobeying orders from the educational authorities, improper management, and confirmed by investigation; D. Immoral behavior, tarnishing the teaching profession; E. Physical or mental defects. (Article 11) These measures will be implemented by the Jiangsu Provincial Education Department after announcement.

Local News

### The Municipal Education Bureau Adds Central Tutorial Schools

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, regarding tutorial schools, has seen a particularly enthusiastic response from students since their expansion last year. Starting this year, one central tutorial school each for workers and peasants will be added, and experienced individuals in education and agriculture/industry will be appointed as principals of each school, tasked with planning school affairs and guiding various tutorial schools, in order to achieve the practical effect of improving tutorial education in Shanghai.

### Da Xia University's New Campus Completed and Relocated

Da Xia University previously purchased more than 150 mu of land next to Zhongshan Road, Fanwangdu, and started construction of a new campus in the spring, as reported in this newspaper several times. It is now heard that the first phase of construction of the school has been completed in stages. The completed buildings include one classroom building, three dormitories for male and female students, three dining halls, one bathroom, and one auditorium. All necessary school equipment is newly purchased. The old campus and all the equipment on Jiaozhou Road will be allocated for the use of the university's affiliated middle school. The relocation will take place at the end of this month, and the new school will open for registration on September 11th. However, during the first week of September, the office and registration location for new students will still be at the old campus on Jiaozhou Road. New dormitories for male and female students are scheduled to be occupied on September 8th. Those arriving in Shanghai before the 8th will temporarily stay in the old dormitories on Jiaozhou Road or Xiaoshadu Road. Fees will be collected starting September 5th. The school will also have two Da Xia public buses running between the new campus and Nicheng Bridge, passing through Baker Road, Avenue Road, Jiaozhou Road, Robison Road, Caojiadu, and Brenan Road, exclusively for the use of the school's faculty, staff and students.

### Recent News of Peiming Girls' Middle School

Peiming Girls' Middle School on Macgregor Road in this city has been established for many years and has achieved excellent results. The school has seen a very enthusiastic response from new students. The existing school buildings will be insufficient for the next semester, and a new school building is now being opened nearby, specifically for the use of the primary school section.

First Act of the Rotary Cup Semifinals

### China Wins Two Singles Matches

Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai win straight sets against Portugal

England and America each win a singles match... England forfeits one group

Today's doubles match... China vs. Portugal... England vs. America

The Shanghai International Tennis Rotary Cup semifinals started yesterday afternoon at 4:30 PM at the China Tennis Court. The matches were two groups of singles matches between China and Portugal and England and America. However, since England's second singles player forfeited to England, only three groups of singles matches were actually played. Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai of China each won straight sets against Canavero and Kosa of Portugal. As a result, China won two singles matches. England's White also defeated America's Smith three sets to zero. At the same time, England also forfeited one group, resulting in England and America each winning one group. Starting at 4:00 PM today, there will be one group each of doubles matches between China and Portugal and England and America. The results of yesterday's three group matches are recorded below:

### Lin Baohua Shows Strength

Lin Baohua's opponent, the Portuguese Canavero, is one of the famous doubles experts at sea. His singles skills are far from his doubles stability. However, it is not because of his lack of knowledge, but because of his lack of physical strength. At the beginning of the fierce battle, the old general wielded his sword and rode his horse, and was indeed a hero for a while. He won the first game. Lin Baohua's technique is pure and he has a plan in mind. He already knows the opponent's strengths and weaknesses, so in the advance and retreat, high slices, low nets, forward draws, and counterattacks, he directly hit the enemy's vital points. After losing the first game, he won the next three games in a row. He finally won the first set 6-3. In the second set, Lin's ball momentum was even stronger, and Canavero's response became more and more poor. Soon Lin won again 6-1. In the third set, Canavero's ambition broke out and he was unwilling to fall behind, struggling several times and making every effort. Lin initially planned to go straight in and complete the great cause, but considering the opponent's stubbornness, he turned into a tense situation. The final victory of the third set still went to Lin 6-4, but there was indeed a fierce battle in it.

(China) Lin Baohua (6...3 6...1 6...4) Canavero (Portugal)

### Rotary Cup Singles Players from China, Portugal, and England

The posture of the three players hitting the ball (1) English player White (Photo by Wang Kai) (2) Chinese player Lin Baohua (3) Qiu Feihai (Photo by Ye Changlie) (1) Portuguese player Canavero (2) (Photo by Ye Changlie)

### Qiu Feihai Achieves Victory

With steady technique and skillful skills, Qiu Feihai defeated the Portuguese Korasha, making him helpless. Korasha was originally a new genius, good at running and able to withstand battles. This time he met Qiu, and before the battle he had a strategy to try to take advantage of the net and hope for a miracle. Unexpectedly, Qiu's sudden east and west side balls had already made him at a loss. Occasionally, when the time came, he rushed forward to the net, but the rear was empty, and Qiu took the opportunity to enter directly. In short, Korasha had completely revealed all his abilities, but he was eventually overturned by Qiu at will. The first set was 6-0, and the results of the second and third sets were the same. All 18 games in the three sets were under Qiu's control. He won the entire victory in just 40 minutes. It was not a good sight.

(China) Qiu Feihai (6...0 6...0 6...0) Korasha (Portugal)

### White Shows His Skills

The Englishman White, who has dominated the sea for many years in singles, attacked the American Smith yesterday like a storm, making it difficult to resist. The first set was especially his amazing work, winning all with a straight 6. The second set was as strong as ever. Except for the fourth game, when Smith won back a game with a net, the rest all failed. As a result, White won 6-1. In the third set, White, with a 5-1 lead, suddenly showed signs of fatigue and suffered a sudden blow from Smith, losing two games. Fortunately, the difference in skills was too great, so he finally won 6-3. (England) White (6...0 6...1 6...3) Smith (America)

### Individual Skills

Yesterday's three groups of talents were quite different, so they all decided the winner and loser with a one-sided situation. The three winners also had their own strengths. Qiu was steady and mature, with excellent positioning. Lin's serve was powerful and he was good at the net. White's draw and hit were appropriate and the ball was not wasted. Among the three losers, Canavero was the strongest, and the other two were even further apart.

At the same time, England's White and Stokes will fight against America's Sguya and Haines. The victory or defeat of England and America is related to the overall situation in the future, and both sides attach great importance to it. The battle between China and Portugal is relatively relaxed.

### The Main Purpose of the Huadong Sports Company

Striving to encourage various sports

Achieving the goal of promoting domestic goods
