Free Talk

A Laughing Matter

— Hai Ke

Man—Darling, if you are willing to marry me, I would be happy even if I died.

Woman—Saving a life is better than building a seven-story pagoda. That's why I don't want to marry you.

A—Why have there been so many divorce cases lately? Everyone is treating it like a daily meal. What is the reason for this? It's worth studying.

B—It's very simple. It's because there are too many people getting married.

Father—When I was your age, I never smoked cigarettes. In the future, when you have a son, you won't be able to teach him a lesson.

Son—Father, I am the most easygoing person. I won't be as pretentious as you are.

A—What do you think of the article I just wrote?

B—What are you talking about?

A—Haven't you read it yet?

B—I've read it. That's why I'm asking you this.

Mother—Child, where did the piece of cake in my plate go?

Son—Mother, I gave it to a starving child.

Mother—You're so young and you already know how to do good deeds. I will never blame you. But what about that poor child?

Son—Here it is. It's me.

Small Talk by the Autumn Window

— Zhi Zheng

The early autumn day is long. Living in a quiet room, I occasionally recall anecdotes of contemporary people. I will select a few to help with conversation.

Wu Zhihui on the Street Wu Zhihui, after mediating the war without results, retired to Shanghai. He lived in seclusion. One day, I went to Shilu, Damalu, for some matters. Suddenly, I saw Mr. Wu walking slowly north. He was wearing an old Hangzhou silk long gown and white shoes. He frequently wiped the sweat from his forehead with a handkerchief. At that time, Shilu was crowded with people. Mr. Wu went to various clothing stores, standing for a few minutes, paying attention to the clothes hanging there. Because Mr. Wu looked like a country person, no one recognized him. I originally intended to be Mr. Wu's follower for five minutes, to observe the behavior of a great man. Unfortunately, I couldn't because of matters. I still regret it to this day.

Song Ziwen at the Train Station Finance Minister Song Ziwen, strategizing and planning, has worked hard and made great contributions. But I have never been able to see his demeanor. One morning, I was at the train station for some matters. Suddenly, I saw armed military police, distributed at important points. They drew their guns from their holsters, as if under martial law. For a time, the air was unusually tense. Then a soldier carrying a machine gun patrolled back and forth. The pedestrians became more and more suspicious. While I was surprised, a car entered the station. The soldiers rushed forward to greet him. I saw Minister Song slowly get out of the car. He was wearing a white serge Western suit and a white hat. He was tall and burly. He was wearing glasses. At that time, the military police along the way shouted "Attention!" and raised their hands in salute. Song smiled and answered them.

Li Zhaohuan on a Rickshaw Li Zhaohuan is the Permanent Vice Minister of the Ministry of Railways. He also serves as the Vice President of Jiaotong University. He comes to the school three days a week and spends the rest of the days in Beijing. He travels between Beijing and Shanghai, not shirking his hard work. He comes to the school to work very early every day. Sometimes he only takes a rickshaw. He travels lightly and simply. The public doesn't know that he is the president. It is also heard that although he is the Vice Minister, he is still not married. Chinese people often like to marry early. Some even boast about love when their personal economy is not independent. Looking at Mr. Li, the difference between the worthy and the unworthy is far away.

New Capital, Old Tales

— Li Taoan

There is a certain prominent family in Nanjing. Their surname cannot be verified. They practice the religion of Muhammad and are devout believers. Those who know the history of their ancestors always tell it. Those who hear it are fascinated by its tactful and moving nature.

During the Tongzhi and Guangxu years of the late Qing Dynasty, domestic transportation was not yet developed. Travelers had to rely on boats, carts, and horses to travel. A certain Jia from Anhui lived in Baixia, working as a donkey driver. For many years, he whipped his donkey and held the lantern, running around and following people. He looked extremely tired. But he was very honest and decisive in his dealings. He was good at observing people's expressions and was very popular. A certain new noble, with matters to report, went to the province to meet with the emperor. He left his travel suitcase on the road. The suitcase contained many confidential documents. He searched everywhere but could not find it. He was very worried. He posted notices in the thoroughfares, hoping to get it back. It happened that a certain Jia found it. He immediately returned it to the owner. The owner saw that he was simple and pleasing and appreciated him greatly. He kept him for his own use. Soon, the certain noble opened a government in Jiangnan. His power and position were prominent. Jia also attached himself to the tail of the horse and rose to fame. He rose rapidly. Before long, his mansion was continuous. He was like a great family. At that time, a certain uninhibited celebrity, who had a bumpy life and was not used by the world, had prominent bones and was a strange figure in the literary world. He asked about the events of his humble beginnings. He satirized him with poetry. The poem was passed down in the literary world and spread as a beautiful tale. One sentence said: "Blue feather of the fifth rank hangs the court beads. How majestic and great a man. Do you remember the wind and snow on Ba Bridge? Waving the whip and calling Du Du." The end said Du Du, which is onomatopoeic. It captures the spirit perfectly. The words are especially humorous but not abusive. They express the ability to tease, anger, laugh, and scold to the fullest. When a certain Jia heard it, he could do nothing about it. He just smiled it off.

After Reading Hu Zijing's Book

— He An

Changsha was burned and killed by the Communist bandits, creating an unprecedented catastrophe. The reports carried before on the killing of Mr. Hu Zijing. Yesterday I suddenly met him in Hanyang. I asked about everything. I learned that because he had just returned from mourning his wife and was unable to take on the position, he strongly declined the presidency of Hunan University. He did not avoid the turmoil in advance and was trapped in the city. The rumors arose because of this. Mr. Hu founded Mingde School in the Gui Mao year of the previous Qing Dynasty. It has been 28 years since then. He has been running around for school funds and has spared no effort. He is honest and upright. He does not take anything improperly. He has no private savings. Society respects him for this. Because Mr. Hu has gained the sympathy of society, he is still running around at the age of 60, not knowing that his old age is coming. He cannot be compared with Ye Dehui, who is arrogant and does not follow the rules. When Mingde was first founded, it was a middle school. Later, it was a normal elementary school and a higher elementary school. In the second year of the Republic of China, a university was established in Beijing. In the eighth year, another university was established in Hankou, planning to move to Beiping. In the fourteenth year, it was closed due to insufficient funds. In Changsha, he focused on running the middle school and greatly expanded it. After the establishment of the National Government, he was rewarded. Last August, the Hunan government hired him as the president of Hunan University. It was near the start of school. He came out to maintain it. For a year, he deeply felt that he could not take care of both. He still wanted to focus all his efforts on maintaining Mingde and carrying out his original intention of hard work and sincerity. He Yunqiao and Mr. Hu have no teacher-student relationship and rarely meet. His position at Hunan University was not because of He Yunqiao personally, but to do his best for education in Hunan. Mr. Hu has never engaged in political life for decades. Everyone in the country knows this. To say that he took the position of president in his later years to seek the position of provincial affairs officer is even more inappropriate. Those who know Mr. Hu will laugh. He An has known Mr. Hu for the longest time. When Mr. Hu was raising money in Nanyang, I helped him. From this, I know the matter very well. Many of the sections recorded by Mr. Fang Er are inconsistent. Therefore, I specially add to the book, and I also show that Mr. Hu is well, to show those in the country who know Mr. Hu.

A Trip to the Four Caves of Hangzhou

— He Haisheng, sent from Hangzhou

Hangzhou's famous scenery is the best in the world. Throughout the years, Chinese and foreign men and women come to visit, endlessly. It is almost like being on the Shanyin Road. A few days ago, a friend named Chi Chu came to my house and invited me to visit the Yellow Dragon Cave. It was a cloudy day, as if it would rain. Chi Chu urged me to go. I was afraid of rain along the way and hesitated. Chi Chu said resolutely, "Why don't we take a risk and go?" I followed him. So I put on my clothes and went out together. We took a public bus to Guanyin Station. After getting off the bus, we walked for about three miles.

Yellow Dragon Cave As we approached the door, we saw two ponds on both sides. Further in, there was a pavilion and beautiful houses. There were rockeries all around, exquisite and delicate. There were three tiger mouths on them. Clear springs flowed down. We admired it endlessly. But the cave was still above. So we climbed the steps. After a few dozen steps, there was a Qianlong imperial stele. After a while, we reached our destination. We went straight into the Yellow Dragon. There was nothing in the cave, only piles of rocks. We wandered around for a while and then went down. After coming out, we climbed again.

Purple Cloud Cave The trees along the road reached the sky. Soon we reached the entrance of the cave. Above it was a plaque that said "Cave Heaven Scenic Spot." There were three Buddhas in the cave. Foolish men and women worshiped them. Next to it was the Seven Star Spring. It was dark and nothing could be seen. There were stone benches for guests to sit on. The light was more sufficient than in the Yellow Dragon Cave. Although the exterior was not as good, the interior was better. Chi Chu and I sat down and ate the cakes and pastries we brought to fill our stomachs. But our interest in traveling was not over. We went to visit

Bat Cave There were thousands of bats, gathering inside. The smell was unbearable. Moreover, there was no way to enter the cave. We covered our noses and passed by. We changed our visit to

Golden Drum Cave This is a relic of the Song Dynasty. It is said that Taoists often heard the sound of bells and drums at that time. They searched for it but could not find it. So they named it that way. It is a absurd saying, which seems credible but cannot be fully believed. Outside there is a statue of Lao Tzu. On the right side is a very small cave. It is full of water. The depth of the abyss cannot be measured. There is nothing else to record. When we returned, Chi Chu said proudly, "Today we should drink to celebrate the success of our adventure." So we had a drink at a tavern and parted ways. (With gratitude)

On Cats

— Wu Tianni

The nature of cats is gentle and active. They like to live near people. However, if taught properly, they can be useful in some ways. It's just that their intelligence is far inferior to that of dogs. Many young ladies in the country like to keep them, but men rarely accept them. However, the following few points cannot be generalized.

Years ago, my family had a special dog named Lingling. It was of a very good breed, but unfortunately, it had become mixed. Its color was pure black and it was quite small. When it was time to find a mate, it was difficult to find a female dog of the same size. Coincidentally, we had a female cat that was as big as the dog. Suddenly, the dog had a strange idea and often snuggled up to the cat, showing great affection. Ordinary cats are afraid of dogs, but this cat was perfectly at ease. Sometimes it would raise its tail and meow loudly, letting the dog do whatever it wanted. However, cats and dogs are different, and it was difficult for them to truly be together. The mess they left behind was quite laughable. The cat was completely white and became pregnant the following year, giving birth to a pure black kitten. This was definitely not from the dog. But the mother cat was completely white, and the kitten was pure black like a dog, which was also a strange thing. There are truly some unbelievable things in the world. As the kitten grew up, it became very familiar with Lingling. Lingling also loved it very much and would often lie in the doghouse with it. After several months, both the cat and the dog grew up, and their love was as strong as before. But I have been away from my hometown for many years, and I don't know what they are like now.

My aunt, Madam Zhou, is the mother of Meige from Jingzhou. She is a devout Buddhist. She has a Buddhist hall at home, which is very clean. One day, a cat gave birth to a litter on the altar in front of the Buddha. The family thought it was disrespectful to the Buddha, so they moved the kittens to a basket behind the door while the mother cat was away. Unexpectedly, after being moved, the mother cat refused to recognize her kittens. No matter how hard they tried to make her feed them, she ignored them. Now, there are five kittens in total. They have only been born for three days and have been crying all night, starving and waiting to die. Alas, what have they done to deserve this tragedy? I wonder if any readers have a way to make the mother cat change her mind and feed her kittens again.

A Brief Account of the Two Major Expositions in Belgium (Part 2)

— Liu Zeng, sent from Paris

Antwerp is the cultural center of northwestern Belgium, facing Liège, the cultural center of the southeast. The residents speak the Flamanp language, which is similar to Dutch and German. The nature of the Antwerp Exposition is different from that of the Liège Exposition. It is mainly focused on products from various colonies. China has no colonies and is seeking not to become a colony of others, which is impossible. Of course, we are not qualified to participate in this exposition.

The largest participating countries are France, England, Japan, the Netherlands, and Italy. Each country has built huge buildings to display the harvests of their colonies.

What Chinese visitors find most heartbreaking is the Japanese propaganda about South Manchuria. The purpose of the Japanese participation in this exposition is to promote South Manchuria as their colony to various countries. Therefore, Korea, Taiwan, Ryukyu, and other places are of secondary importance in this exposition. The main focus is South Manchuria. The Japanese have built a special pavilion, full of photos of South Manchuria, statistical tables, and specimens of soybeans and peanuts produced there. In the photos, Chinese people are mostly wearing long robes and melon-shaped hats, being directed by Japanese people in Western suits. According to their statistical tables, South Manchuria now produces 4.6 million tons of soybeans annually, three-quarters of which are used to meet the needs of Europeans. There is also a map showing South Manchuria and Japan painted in the same color. This South Manchurian pavilion also has a lacquered couplet that reads, "Scholars, farmers, artisans, and merchants gather in this room," "Gathering the grand sights of the southeast, northwest, and north." The inscription reads "Respectfully presented by Dong Annan Shu Jun, wishing the Great French Empire ten thousand years." Chinese characters are used to sing the praises of the people of a fallen country. Is this not lamentable?

Leaving the Japanese pavilion and entering the French pavilion, there are also things that make people sigh. In addition to doing their best to promote the success of non-colonialism, France has also set up a special room to boast about its achievements in invading the yellow race. This room is the Annam Pavilion. Annam has no special culture of its own. All it has is inherited from China. Therefore, the items on display in the Annam Pavilion are all similar to Chinese items. Each door in the pavilion has a gold-lacquered couplet. The one in the center reads, "The Eastern Sea prays three times, and pearls and jade have always been abundant," "French grace covers the four borders, and wealth and industry compete to open." The inscription reads, "Respectfully presented by Dong Annan Shu Jun, wishing the Great French Empire ten thousand years." Chinese characters are only used by the people of a fallen country to sing praises. Is this not deplorable?

There are many other noteworthy things, but due to the limited space in this newspaper, they are all omitted. In short, according to the reporter's personal opinion, our country had no need to participate in this exposition. (The United States, Germany, and other countries did not participate.) If we want to participate, we should participate on a large scale and with a plan. We should study the psychology of Westerners and pay attention to scientific methods in the selection and display of exhibits, so that in addition to promoting national quintessence, it can also help promote foreign trade.

Correction: The last four lines of yesterday's article should have been placed before the section "Southern Venue..." We hereby correct this.

Warmth in the Heart (260)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 13: Who Unintentionally Plants Fortune and Gains a Diamond Ring? Only This Karma Sings the Golden Thread with Intent

This day, because there were many guests, the hosts were inevitably a little busy. But the other four hosts were fine. Ling Zhixiang was the host of hosts today, and he was even busier, at a loss for what to do. Everyone had to ask this young master Ling about everything. But he found it very interesting. When it came time to drink, he insisted on setting up ten tables of wine at the same time. When it came time to call for entertainment, it was a chaotic scene with flowers flying and branches shaking. When the entertainers arrived, it was even more of a clamor. With seventy or eighty guests, each calling for an entertainer, there were seventy or eighty people. And Ling Zhixiang declared that the more entertainers called, the better. Each person had to call for at least two entertainers. It truly became a scene of "ten thousand people leaving their alleys to celebrate the new dress." All the famous courtesans of Shanghai's northern district were called out. At this time, next to Zuo Shichen, there was a singer, who was very shy with the guests. He was probably a new performer. The one who accompanied him, however, was a charming and sweet elder sister, who was very responsive to the guests and handled everything with ease. It seemed that she had been trained in the brothel, unlike those who came from the countryside. Zuo Shichen thought that even in a brothel, there was economic use of talent. For example, this singer was an outstanding talent. It didn't matter if the person accompanying him was a little less talented. He wouldn't even mind if an old woman came along. If the singer couldn't attract guests, then a supporting talent was indispensable. Especially for newly debuted prostitutes, they relied on a good elder sister to guide them at all times. In the imperial era, when the emperor was young, he relied on several virtuous and loyal ministers to be his teachers and advisors to assist the young ruler. That was the same principle. Zuo Shichen thought this way in his heart, and couldn't help but look over there frequently. He felt that the elder sister who accompanied the entertainer looked somewhat familiar. When she saw Zuo Shichen looking at her, she smiled back at him. The people who accompanied the entertainers used to stand there. Because her position was very close to Zuo Shichen, she walked over and said, "Are you Mr. Zuo? Are you the second young master Zuo?" Zuo Shichen was stunned and said, "How do you know?" She smiled and said, "Don't you remember? I saw you in Cuiyun's room before." When Zuo Shichen heard this, he vaguely remembered, but he couldn't call out her name. So he asked, "What's the name of the entertainer you're accompanying now?" But she didn't answer this question. Instead, she asked Zuo Shichen, "Cuiyun has come out. Have you called her?" Zuo Shichen said, "Really? I didn't know at all. Is she still called Cuiyun? Where is she?" She said, "Her name has been changed to Channong. She's at Baihuadi." Zuo Shichen took a piece of entertainment ticket in his hand and said, "How is it written?" She said, "Chan is the Chan character in the Buddhist and Taoist ceremony. Nong is the Nong character in Wang Xiaonong." Zuo Shichen said, "What a good name, Channong. Who gave her this name?" She said, "I heard that the third elder sister gave it to herself."

Consequently, this manufacturer re-entered the cotton futures market, increasing their holdings, purchasing four to five thousand bales over two days. Short covering occurred, causing the market to become volatile and slightly rise. Distant months were also affected.

Hankow Standard was weak in the morning but strengthened in the afternoon. At the opening of the morning session, the market sentiment was extremely weak, following the decline of foreign cotton by 2.5 to 3 mace. In the afternoon, due to the current month's influence, distant months rose, slightly strengthening the market. The current month rose by 5 mace, and distant months rose by 2.5 mace. The total daily trading volume was 57,600 bales. Sales included 3,300 bales by Shenchang, 2,200 bales by Qinfeng, 1,900 bales each by Dachangcheng and Maoji, 1,800 bales by Lichang, and 1,200 to 1,900 bales each by Yichang, Taichang, Yukang, Tianchang, Jinfeng, Xiesheng, Dafu, Daji, and Taixing. Purchases included 1,200 bales by Hengda, 3,000 bales by Changji, 2,900 bales by Yuda, 5,300 bales by Taixing, and 3,300 bales by Yiyu, and 2,400 bales by Dafeng. The closing prices for Hankow Standard are recorded on the left.

Statistics on China's Cotton Industry in the First Half of the Year

Increasing Number of Spindles… Growing Imports of Foreign Cotton

The China Merchants Yarn Factory Association recently released the following statistics on the transfer of spindles and consumption and inventory of raw cotton by various spinning mills in the first half of this year (raw cotton inventory and consumption are measured in units of 500-pound bales):

Raw Cotton Consumption This Year, First Half Last Year, Second Half Raw Cotton Inventory This Year, First Half Last Year, Second Half

Chinese Cotton 770785 762017 226796 246750

American Cotton 161520 129647 58415 44600

Indian Cotton 164218 198746 128975 51288

Egyptian Cotton 1584 861 1420 1637

Other 5166 1251 950 482

Total 1203273 1092522 416556 344757

Spindle Count ▲Suspended Operation

Actual Operating Count 3827900 3699402

Number of Suspended Spindles 448416 565831

Under Construction 200950 180940

Hours Suspended 1320 1837

Weeks Suspended 1.25 2.13

Observing the above statistics, two points are worth noting: (1) China's spinning industry is gradually progressing, and (2) the demand for foreign cotton is increasing. China's spinning industry has been relatively successful since the year before last, and there have been frequent reports of adding spindles and establishing factories. Although it has been slightly affected recently by exchange rate fluctuations, as of the end of June, the actual number of spindles operating (referring to yarn spindles; thread spindles and waste cotton spindles are not included) was 3,827,900, with 200,950 spindles under installation, bringing the total to nearly 4 million. The actual number of spindles operating has increased by more than 128,000 compared to the end of last year. If politics become more stable, the future prospects are promising. However, it should be noted that Japanese merchants account for 39% of this number, and British merchants account for a little over 4%. It is hoped that the government and the people will maintain and promote its development to prevent the continued growth of foreign commercial power.

During the first half of the year, the consumption of raw cotton increased with the increase in yarn spindles, but the increase rate of foreign cotton was greater than that of Chinese cotton, and the same is true for inventories. This has a significant impact on China's cotton production. It is found that China's cotton production in recent years has been approximately 5 to 6 million bales, which is far from sufficient to meet the consumption of spinning mills. Moreover, the quality is coarse and short, making it unsuitable for fine spinning. The fiber of Lingbao cotton in Henan Province is relatively fine and long and can be used to spin yarn of 32 counts or higher. However, the quantity is small and there are signs of degradation, so finer yarn must be spun with cotton from the United States and Egypt. The import of foreign cotton is therefore huge. Examining the customs trade register, the import surplus of cotton in recent years has approached 100 million Customs taels. It is truly alarming for a country that relies on agriculture to have such a large import surplus of agricultural products. There is great danger for both agriculture and industry. Therefore, expanding production and improving quality are urgent matters for revitalizing the cotton industry.

Food Prices Plunge in the Rice Market Downriver

Zhabei

Yesterday, the source of inland rice transfers was shifting, and market sales were poor. Although the stock of northern Japonica rice in Shanghai was not large, store inventories were sufficient. Therefore, while top-quality Japonica rice remained at 21 yuan, ordinary Zhongguan rice fell by 2 to 3 jiao. In some cases, the price fell by as much as half a yuan, resulting in a very soft market. The future of Japonica rice prices depends on the lower reaches of the market. Once Western Xin rice is released, the accumulated stock in Changshu and Wuxi will inevitably be sold off. Furthermore, the price of foreign rice has been weak recently, Xiang rice will soon be shipped, and this year's output of Dongxin Japonica rice is expected to be twice as high as in previous years, arriving in Shanghai every morning at around 1,000 shi. Therefore, although the supply of broken Japonica rice in Shanghai is limited, it will not have much impact. Currently, factories are gradually selling off their stocks, causing the market to fall by half a yuan yesterday, opening high at 19 yuan and trending downward. Demand from new customers for top-quality rice was weak, with prices falling by 1 to 2 jiao. Can Yang top-quality rice saw some support,勉開 at around 15 yuan. Shipments of Baiyuan rice increased, but sales were sluggish. Top-quality rice was at a premium of a little over half a jiao, opening at 19.3 to 19.4 yuan. Market expectations were focused on 19 yuan. Across the board, prices of all types of rice plunged sharply yesterday, resulting in a very soft market.

South Shanghai

Prices downriver saw some support, but street sales were weak. The price of northern broken white rice also fell by 3 jiao, and the trend is expected to follow the northern market. Ordinary rice prices hovered around 20 yuan. Incoming shipments of southern thin-husked rice were slightly received but also fell by 1 to 2 jiao, with top-quality rice opening at 20.05 to 20.06 yuan. Demand for Bianyuan rice was weak, with prices generally around the 19 yuan mark.

Foreign Rice: High-Grade Weak, Medium-Grade Popular

Yesterday, secondary rice from the mainland being shipped by agents enlivened the foreign rice market. Transactions of various types of rice, including Da Xiaojiao and Min Dang rice, increased, and prices became more favorable. However, the stock of No. 1 Saigon rice was not large, and digestion was slow, causing the market to move in the opposite direction to that of medium-grade rice. The market opened with 500 bags of No. 1 Saigon rice at 16 yuan to 15.8 yuan, slightly lower than before. 300 bags of No. 2 Saigon rice were priced at 14.16 yuan, 2,000 bags of Xiaojiao rice were priced at 15 yuan to 14.6 yuan, 1,500 bags of Dajiao rice were priced at 12.4 yuan, 60 bags of Hong Dajiao rice were priced at 11.7 to 11.8 yuan, and 60 bags of Min Dang rice were priced at 15.22 to 14.85 yuan, all slightly higher than the previous market.

Flour Market Manipulated by Bulls

Gold Prices Rebound… Short Sellers Must Gradually Cover Positions

Yesterday, the flour market showed another improving trend. Since the current month has been largely absorbed by bullish speculators, the amount of short positions held by insiders is limited. Outside short sellers have no choice but to gradually cover their positions in the face of this forced price increase. Although prices of foreign wheat for distant months have been reported to be down by about 1 to 2 jiao, the gold market has rebounded, which has inevitably influenced sentiment. Given this situation, if demand picks up, the large bullish speculators will inevitably drive prices higher and higher. Otherwise, there will be complaints, and excessive manipulation will likely be avoided. As a result, the current month was up by 1 fen and 2.5 li compared to the previous day, September was up by 1.5 fen, October, December, and January were up by 1 fen, and November was up by 7.5 li.

Wheat Futures Open Higher and Rise Steadily

Yesterday, wheat futures prices continued to rise across the board, especially for the current month. As the current month approaches delivery, the inventory in the market, although estimated to be around 60,000 to 70,000, is mostly medium and secondary grade, with few high-quality goods. Those that meet the exchange's standards are even scarcer. Therefore, the exchange's standard goods are like rare commodities due to delivery requirements. Thus, after the opening price, prices opened higher and rose steadily, creating a short squeeze. September also saw a significant rise due to its proximity to the current month, while distant months remained relatively stable. As a result, the current month was up by 6 fen compared to the previous day, September was up by 4 fen, and October to January were up by 2 fen each. Spot wheat prices fell by 4 to 5 fen because the goods were of medium and secondary quality and did not meet the factory's requirements. More than 4,000 bales of wheat from Xuzhou, Yaowan, Huangqiao, and Niuzhuang were opened and acquired by Fuxin and Fufeng.

Piece Goods: Sales of Both Domestic and Foreign Goods Are Very Quiet

Local Cotton Cloth

Yesterday's market was slightly soft due to the decline in American cotton and the approaching end of August. Fine cloth was down by a small amount of 5 fen, fine twill was down by a small amount of 2.5 fen. There was a shortage of coarse cloth, and definite orders for coarse twill from the Wentaibang were for 50 to 60 pieces. 16-pound Five Yuanbao was sold at 7 taels, 5 mace, and 7.5 fen. 14-pound Ren Ta was sold at 6 taels and 3.5 qian, 11-pound Mao Ya was sold at 5 taels. There were slight transactions of Yihhe bleached cloth from the Jinbang, with Jin Santai at 7 taels and 6 qian, and Yunwai Piaoxiang at 7 taels and 8 qian.

East and West Piece Goods

Actual sales were stagnant as people adopted a wait-and-see approach. Holders of goods had to pay to extend their financing, and the market was weak. The quietness of transactions was rarely seen. Dark-colored and patterned Ting cloth had reached around 9 qian. Shui Lang Rong was down by a small amount of 2.5 li, and Guang Xie was also quite weak. Shile Bird fine cloth fell by 1 qian, selling at 7 taels and 7 qian, and bleached cloth was down by a small amount of 5 fen. Queqiao Hui was at 10 taels and 7 qian, Huaniao was at 7 taels and 3.5 qian, and Shichong was at 7 taels and 7 qian. However, Zhigong Ni and Zhigong Duan remained firm. Western goods, Chongtai Western satin, were added to by the Changjiangbang yesterday, with Sassoon Tianguan at 3 qian and 3.5 fen, and Gongping Jiucai Tong at 3 qian and 3 fen. Thick Zhigong Ni also saw slight movement.

Silk and Tea: Zhenmei Green Tea Sales to England Show Slight Movement

Incoming Zhenmei green tea from the tea estates, Yingzhuang Jinlong, Tianxiang, Duode, and other firms, all had telegraphic transfers yesterday. However, because the initial orders were extended, the market price fell by 5 to 6 taels. Items such as Zhenmei Zhucha also saw some scattered transactions, with no price increases or decreases. The most important issue, the sale of Chinese tea to Russia, was previously suspended due to the arrest of a tea agent in Hankou. Yesterday, a telegraphic dispatch from Hankou stated that the military authorities in Wuhan had agreed to release the Russian agent, and tea sales seemed unaffected.

North-South Goods: Lower-Grade Guangdong Lychees Open with Tight Prices

Lower-grade Guangdong lychees have recently seen a lively market and firm prices. Yesterday, new goods were opened on the market. Shuidong lychees opened at over 16 taels, selected Zhuang lychees opened at around 13 taels, and those below that opened at around 11 taels, all up by about 2 taels compared to the previous low prices. Since the prices are relatively affordable and easy to sell, the market price is trending upward despite the large supply.

Social News

Chilean Government Undertakes Abolition of the Death Penalty

Submitting a new criminal law proposal to the National Congress, working hard for the happiness of children

According to the World News Agency, the New York-published "Chile" monthly magazine reports that the Chilean government has recently drafted a new criminal law proposal and submitted it to the National Congress. The content of the new criminal law is entirely based on new concepts of criminal law science and the scientific progress of psychology, sociology, and biology. The aim is to abolish the death penalty and life imprisonment, focusing on crime prevention rather than punishment. The sentencing of an offender places great emphasis on considering their personal background and environment. The criminal laws of countries such as Switzerland, Germany, and Sweden were used as blueprints during the drafting process. Among the innovative provisions are: (1) Fines are determined based on the offender's income and economic obligations; (2) Imprisonment periods are not fixed, but rather flexible based on the offender's ability to reform; (3) The culpability of accomplices is equal to that of the perpetrators. Regarding the implementation of this new criminal law, the Chilean government has established a major prison reform plan, which is currently underway. This includes the construction of modern new prison buildings, improvement of prison procedures, and the scientific management of prisons.

The monthly magazine also reports that from July 4th to 11th, Peru held the Sixth Pan-American Child Conference. Chile made significant contributions to this conference. Chile is currently engaged in extensive improvements to the well-being of children, with particular emphasis on addressing the issue of juvenile delinquency. There are regulations for maternity benefits for nursing mothers, and the National Child Welfare Association has established free milk distribution agencies in various locations to specifically donate to mothers from poor families. In the past six months of the year, the milk distribution stations in Santiago have nourished 1,293 children, with medical assistance provided in 14,362 cases. Every elementary school in the country has a doctor who enforces compulsory medical treatment for students to improve their health. The handling of juvenile delinquency is now being improved using scientific methods. Old-fashioned orphanages are now being replaced by social group-style remedial education institutions. These educational institutions contain a family atmosphere to help children forget the pain of being orphaned.

Europe and America Enter an Era of Large-Scale Ship Layups

Europe: 6 Million Tons; America: Over 200 Vessels

Last year, the European shipping industry had virtually no ship layups. However, between last winter and this spring, due to a sharp drop in freight rates, Europe began to have substantial ship layups in January of this year, with the number confirmed to be 100,000 tons. By February, it had reached 500,000 tons; in March, it reached 1 million tons; and in April, it increased to 3 million tons. It now exceeds 6 million tons. This means that approximately 15% of Europe's current 40 million tons of shipping capacity is laid up.

Furthermore, according to Captain Jones of the Prince Line's China Prince, there are currently over 200 ships laid up in America. Along the Atlantic coast, these ships are lying empty, awaiting orders, presenting a strange spectacle reminiscent of a grand naval review.

Submarine Exhibition Opens in Tokyo, Japan

Displaying Records of the Sino-Japanese War

Tokyo Dispatch: With the initiation of former Councilor Arima Yushou in Tokyo, a submarine exhibition is currently being held at the Matsuya Department Store in Ginza, scheduled to run until the end of the month. The exhibition hall displays cross-sections of submarines, the radio equipment and cooking facilities inside submarines, over a hundred items including records of the Sino-Japanese War by Navy Captain Hirose Hikota, and popular materials on the origins and course of the Russo-Japanese War. The rooftop command tower also features periscopes, and the central front of the entrance is decorated with models of aircraft carriers taking off and landing, and submarines diving. The cost of the equipment and setup is 15,000 yuan.

"Caoye" Poetry Special Issue Published

"Caoye Weekly" Volume 3, Number 5, published by the "Caoye" Society at 34 Filun Road, is a special issue dedicated to poetry. It contains eleven poems and over a dozen literary news items, all of which are powerful and filled with nationalism. Examples include Wang Tiehua's "Whipping the Horse Forward" and "Symphony of the Streams," Tang Zenghuang's "Hymn" and "Era's Praise, That Youth," Huanghun's "The Uneasy Gradually River," Zhang Xiamei's "Forward," and Baina's "Offering to the Soldiers." It is available for sale at newspaper vendors, school gatehouses, and so on.

Ministry of Education of Japan Possesses 40,000 Volumes

3,000 Missing Books Found

Tokyo Dispatch: A major panic has broken out within the Ministry of Education of Japan. Since the earthquake, the Ministry has purchased approximately 40,000 books annually, freely lending them out to various departments for the use of staff. Recently, while organizing the purchase ledgers, it was discovered that approximately 3,000 books were missing. Most of these are expensive Western books that are difficult for individuals to obtain, with a total value exceeding ten thousand yuan. The Expenditure Section, due to the unexpected nature of the incident, is currently conducting a more detailed investigation. The cause of the missing books appears to be that they were borrowed and left at home, and then forgotten to be returned due to personnel transfers and dismissals, etc. It is also suspected that some intentionally took them home with no intention of returning them. The Ministry will soon hold a meeting to discuss a solution.

The Huiluo Company on Nanjing Road and Sichuan Road announced that, due to the renovation of its storefront, the company held a large-scale discount sale for one month. Now that the period has expired, all the remaining stock from the discount sale, in various colors, is available. To give preferential treatment to customers, all items are now included in the one-yuan goods section. For example, fountain pens with platinum nibs, with smooth tips that never leak, and exceptionally beautiful barrels, cannot be compared to fountain pens on the market that cost over ten yuan apiece. They are now sold for one yuan, so students are flocking to buy them. Other items such as baby clothes in various colors, strongly scented soaps (one yuan can buy a dozen), various silk ties, shagreen bags, various cheongsam materials for autumn, etc., are all included in the one-yuan goods section.

The China Business Advertising Company announced that the Ford Motor Company of America's Dirulu Factory, on the orders of factory owner Henry Ford, has dispatched representative Mr. Collins to China to investigate market conditions in order to determine a strategy for expanding business. Mr. Collins stayed in Shanghai for two weeks, receiving numerous invitations to banquets from Chinese and Western business circles. He was deeply impressed with Shanghai and its neighboring areas, considering them to be excellent opportunities for expanding business now and in the future. He has now left Shanghai for the three northeastern provinces and important northern cities for investigation. He is expected to return to Shanghai around the beginning of September. It is reported that Ford has decided to purchase land near Shanghai to build a new factory to engage in car assembly. A part of the plan can be realized in early September. Because Ford intends to build a very large-scale automobile general factory in China, and Shanghai is considered by Mr. Collins to be the most suitable location for the establishment of the first factory in the general factory.

The bookstore publishes school books such as "An Outline of the History of Chinese Literature," "An Evolutionary History of Chinese Literature," "An Outline of the Evolutionary History of Society," and "The History of the Chinese Revolution," which are well-written and have long been praised by the education community. During the discount period, schools can also receive special discounts for bulk purchases. Discounted book lists are printed and will be sent upon request.

Theater News

The Star Film Company announces that the film actress Xuan Jinglin, a genius beyond compare, is returning to the silver screen. All those who cherish domestically produced films cannot help but rejoice that there is one more talented person in the field of domestic films. Her first film, "Romantic Woman," features Xuan as a romantic woman, and her expressions are so fluent and vivid that they surpass her previous starring roles by far. The film has now been completed and will be released in Shanghai early next month. Recently, the company has also specially written a play for Ms. Xuan, entitled "The Virtuous Mother from the Brothel," in which Xuan plays the virtuous mother, perfectly suited to her role. There is no one who could be more fitting. Xia Peizhen, a newly emerging female star with dramatic talent, will co-star as Xuan's beloved daughter. This play depicts the love between mother and daughter with profound emotion and is further enhanced by the joint performance of these two major stars. It will undoubtedly become one of the most outstanding domestic films. It is currently being actively filmed under the direction of Cheng Shigaoyunyun.

The Flying Eagle Film Company announces that their film "The Tragic Case of a Woman," starring Chen Lianfang, Zha Ruineng, and He Zhigang, is premiering today at the New Central Cinema. The plot briefly describes a dancer, Huang, who, having received higher education, falls into the profession of a dancer due to changes in her environment. She gradually becomes involved in a complex love triangle, and the river of love suddenly erupts into a storm of jealousy, leading to the tragic death of the young dancer. This play depicts the ease with which young women fall into vanity, warns against the dangers of improper love affairs, and strongly condemns the misconduct of wicked young men. The first half of the film is similar to a recent case of a dancer taking poison that occurred in Shanghai, while the second half incorporates a complex detective plot to arouse the audience's interest, and so on.
